                <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1"> vamanadravyāṇāṃ phalādīnāṃ madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni
                        bhavanti | atha madanapuṣpāṇāmātapapariśuṣkāṇāṃ cūrṇaprakuñjaṃ
                        pratyakpuṣpāsadāpuṣpīnimbakaṣāyāṇāmanyatamenāloḍya madhusaindhavayuktāṃ
                        puṣpacūrṇamātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanaśalāṭucūrṇānyevaṃ vā
                        bakularamyakopayuktāni madhulavaṇayuktānyabhiprataptāni;
                        madanaśalāṭucūrṇasiddhāṃ vā tilataṇḍulayavāgūm | nirvṛttānāṃ vā
                        nātiharitapāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvabaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavabu(tu)ṣamudgamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭarātroṣitaklinnabhinnānāṃ phalānāṃ
                        phalapippalīruddhṛtyātape śoṣayet, tāsāṃ
                        dadhimadhupalalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānāmantarnakhamuṣṭimuṣṇe
                        yaṣṭīmadhukakaṣāye kovidārādīnāmanyatame vā kaṣāye pramṛdya rātriparyuṣitaṃ
                        madhusaindhavayuktamāśīrbhirabhimantritamudaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukhamāturaṃ
                        pāyayedanena mantreṇābhimantrya-
                        “brahmadakṣāśvirudrendrabhūcandrārkānalānilāḥ| ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhīgrāmā
                        bhūtasaṅghāśca pāntu te ||1|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.2"> rasāyanamivarṣīṇāṃ devānāmamṛtaṃ yathā |
                        sudhevottamanāgānāṃ bhaiṣajyamidamastu te ||2|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3">viśeṣeṇa śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvidradhiṣu;
                        apravartamāne vā doṣe pippalīvacāgaurasarṣapakalkonmiśraiḥ
                        salavaṇairuṣṇāmbubhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ pravartayedāsamyagvāntalakṣaṇāditi |
                        madanaphalamajjacūrṇaṃ vā tatkvāthaparibhāvitaṃ madanaphalakaṣāyeṇa;
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payasaḥ santānikāṃ kṣaudrayuktāṃ ,
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhaṃ vā payaḥ, madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā
                        yavāgūm, adhobhāgāsṛkpittahṛddāhayoḥ; madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso
                        dadhibhāvamupagatasya dadhyuttaraṃ dadhi vā
                        kaphaprasekacchardimūrcchātamakeṣu; madanaphalamajjarasaṃ snehaṃ vā
                        bhallātakasnehavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet, ātapapariśuṣkaṃ vā tameva
                        jīvantīkaṣāyeṇa, pitte kaphasthānagate; madanaphalamajjakvāthaṃ vā
                        pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ, taccūrṇaṃ vā nimbarūpikākaṣāyayoranyatareṇa
                        santarpaṇakaphajavyādhiharaṃ, madanaphalamajjacūrṇaṃ vā
                        madhūkakāśmaryadrākṣākaṣāyeṇa | madanaphalavidhānamuktam ||3||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4"> jīmūtakakusumacūrṇaṃ pūrvavadeva kṣīreṇa, nirvṛtteṣu
                        kṣīrayavāgūṃ, romaśeṣu santānikāṃ, aromaśeṣu dadhyuttaraṃ, haritapāṇḍuṣu
                        dadhi, tatkaṣāyasaṃsṛṣṭāṃ vā surāṃ kaphārocakakāsaśvāsapāṇḍurogayakṣmasu;
                        paryāgateṣu madanaphalamajjavadupayogaḥ ||4|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5"> tadvadeva kuṭajaphalavidhānam ||5|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"> kṛtavedhanānāmapyeṣa eva kalpaḥ ||6|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7"> ikṣvākukusumacūrṇaṃ vā pūrvavat , evaṃ kṣīreṇa,
                        kāsaśvāsacchardikapharogeṣūpayogaḥ ||7|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8"> dhāmārgavasyāpi madanaphalamajjavadupayogaḥ; viśeṣatastu
                        garagulmodarakāsaśvāsaśleṣmāmayeṣu vāyau ca kaphasthānagate ||8|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9"> kṛtavedhanaphalapippalīnāṃ vamanadravyakaṣāyaparipītānāṃ
                        bahuśaścūrṇamutpalādiṣu dattamāghrātaṃ vāmayati, tattvanavabaddhadoṣeṣu
                        yavāgūmākaṇṭhātpītavatsu ca vidadhyāt |
                        vamanavirecanaśirovirocanadravyāṇyevaṃ vā pradhānatamāni bhavanti ||9|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.10"> bhavataścātra- vamanadravyayogāṇāṃ digiyaṃ samprakīrtitā
                        | tān vibhajya yathāvyādhi kālaśaktiviniścayāt ||10|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.11">kaṣāyaiḥ svarasaiḥ kalkaiścūrṇairapi ca buddhimān |
                        peyalehyādyabhojyeṣu vamanānyupakalpayet ||11|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyo nāma tricatvāriṃśattamo'dhyāyaḥ ||43|| </l>
                </div>
                <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.3"> aruṇābhaṃ trivṛnmūlaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mūlavirecane | pradhānaṃ
                        tilvakastvakṣu phaleṣvapi harītakī ||3|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.4"> taileṣveraṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ svarase kāravellikā | sudhāpayaḥ
                        payaḥsūktamiti prādhānyasaṅgrahaḥ | teṣāṃ vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi
                        yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ||4|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.5"> vairecanadravyarasānupītaṃ mūlaṃ mahattraivṛtamastadoṣam
                        | cūrṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavanāgarāḍhyamamlaiḥ pibenmārutarogajuṣṭaḥ ||5|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.6"> ikṣorvikārairmadhurai rasaistat paitte gade kṣīrayutaṃ
                        pibecca |6| guḍūcyariṣṭatriphalārasena savyoṣamūtraṃ kaphaje pibettat ||6|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.7"> trivarṇakatryūṣaṇayuktametadguḍena lihyādanavena cūrṇam |
                        prasthe ca tanmūlarasasya datvā tanmūlakalkaṃ kuḍavapramāṇam ||7|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.8"> karṣonmite saindhavanāgare ca vipācya kalkīkṛtametadadyāt
                        | tatkalkabhāgaḥ samahauṣadhārdhaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayutaśca peyaḥ ||8|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.9"> samāstrivṛnnāgarakābhayāḥ syurbhāgārdhakaṃ pūgaphalaṃ
                        supakvam | viḍaṅgasāro maricaṃ sadāru yogaḥ sasindhūdbhavamūtrayuktaḥ ||9|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.10"> (virecanadravyabhavaṃ tu cūrṇaṃ rasena teṣāṃ bhiṣajā
                        vimṛdya | tanmūlasiddhena ca sarpiṣā''ktaṃ sevyaṃ tadājye guṭikīkṛtaṃ ca
                        ||10||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.11"> guḍe ca pākābhimukhe nidhāya cūrṇīkṛtaṃ samyagidaṃ
                        vipācya | śītaṃ trijātāktamatho vimṛdya yogānurūpā guṭikāḥ prayojyāḥ) ||11|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.12"> vairekīyadravyacūrṇasya bhāgaṃ siddhaṃ sārdhaṃ
                        kvāthabhāgaiścaturbhiḥ | āmṛdnīyāt sarpiṣā tacchṛtena tatkvāthoṣmasveditaṃ
                        sāmitaṃ ca ||12|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.13"> pākaprāpte phāṇite cūrṇitaṃ tat kṣiptaṃ pakvaṃ cāvatārya
                        prayatnāt | śītībhūtā modakā hṛdyagandhāḥ kāryāstvete bhakṣyakalpāḥ samāsāt
                        ||13||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.14"> rasena teṣāṃ paribhāvya mudgān yūṣaḥ
                        sasindhūdbhavasarpiriṣṭaḥ | vairecane'nyairapi vaidalaiḥ syādevaṃ
                        vidadhyādvamanauṣadhaiśca ||14|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.15"> bhittvā dvidhekṣuṃ parilipya kalkaistribhaṇḍijātaiḥ
                        pratibadhya rajjvā | pakvaṃ ca samyak puṭapākayuktyā khādettu taṃ pittagadī
                        suśītam ||15|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.16"> sitājagandhātvakkṣīrīvidārītrivṛtaḥ samāḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.17"> śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyuktaṃ trivṛccūrṇāvacūrṇitam | recanaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.18"> pacellehaṃ sitākṣaudrapalārdhakuḍavānvitam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.80">bhinattyāśveva doṣāṇāṃ rogān hanti ca dustarān |80|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.82">mahāvṛkṣapayaḥ pītairyavāgūstaṇḍulaiḥ kṛtā | pītā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.84">cūrṇaṃ kāmpillakaṃ vā'pi tatpītaṃ guṭikīkṛtam |84|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86.1"> mūtreṇāplāvya saptāhaṃ snuhīkṣīre tataḥ param | kīrṇaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86.2"> kṣīratvakphalamūlānāṃ vidhānaiḥ parikīrtitaiḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.87"> trivṛcchāṇā mitāstisrastisraśca triphalātvacaḥ |
                        viḍaṅgapippalīkṣāraśāṇāstisraśca cūrṇitāḥ ||87|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.88">lihyāt sarpirmadhubhyāṃ ca modakaṃ vā guḍena vā |
                        bhakṣayenniṣparīhārametacchreṣṭhaṃ virecanam ||88|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.89">gulmaṃ plīhodaraṃ kāsaṃ halīmakamarocakam |
                        kaphavātakṛtāṃścānyān vyādhīnetadvyapohati ||89|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.90"> ghṛteṣu taileṣu payaḥsu cāpi madyeṣu mūtreṣu tathā
                        raseṣu | bhakṣyānnalehyeṣu ca teṣu teṣu virecanānyagramatirvidadhyāt ||90|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.91"> kṣīraṃ rasaḥ kalkamatho kaṣāyaḥ śṛtaśca śītaśca tathaiva
                        cūrṇam | kalpāḥ ṣaḍete khalu bheṣajānāṃ yathottaraṃ te laghavaḥ pradiṣṭāḥ
                        ||91|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        virecanadravyavikalpavijñānīyo nāma catuścatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ||44|| </l>
                </div>
                <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3"> pānīyamāntarīkṣamanirdeśyarasamamṛtaṃ jīvanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ
                        dhāraṇamāśvāsajananaṃ
                        śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrānidrādāhapraśamanamekāntataḥ pathyatamaṃ ca
                        ||3|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4"> tadevāvanipatitamanyatamaṃ rasamupalabhate
                        sthānaviśeṣānnadīnadasarastaḍāgavāpīkūpacuṇṭīprasravaṇodbhidavikirakedārapalvalādi
                        ṣu sthāneṣvavasthitamiti ||4|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5"> tatra, ‘lohitakapilapāṇḍunīlapītaśukleṣvavanipradeśeṣu
                        madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyāṇi yathāsaṅkhyamudakāni sambhavanti’ ityeke
                        bhāṣante ||5|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6"> tattu na samyak; pṛthivyādīnāmanyonyānupraveśakṛtaḥ
                        salilaraso bhavatyutkarṣāpakarṣeṇa | tatra, svalakṣaṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        bhūmāvamlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca; ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ madhuraṃ; tejoguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        kaṭukaṃ tiktaṃ ca; vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṣāyam;
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāmavyaktarasam, avyaktaṃ hyākāśamityataḥ; tat
                        pradhānamavyaktarasatvāt, tatpeyamāntarīkṣālābhe ||6|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7"> tatrāntarīkṣaṃ caturvidham | tadyathā- dhāraṃ, kāraṃ,
                        tauṣāraṃ, haimamiti | teṣāṃ dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ, laghutvāt; tat punardvividhaṃ-
                        gāṅgaṃ, sāmudraṃ ceti | tatra gāṅgamāśvayuje māsi prāyaśo varṣati |
                        tayordvayorapi parīkṣaṇaṃ kurvīta- śālyodanapiṇḍamakuthitamavidagdhaṃ
                        rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve bahiṣkurvīta, sa yadi muhūrtaṃ
                        sthitastādṛśa eva bhavati tadā gāṅgaṃ patatītyavagantavyaṃ; varṇānyatve
                        sikthapraklede ca sāmudramiti vidyāt, tannopādeyam | sāmudramapyāśvayuje
                        māsi gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavadbhavati | gāṅgaṃ punaḥ pradhānaṃ, tadupādadītāśvayuje
                        māsi | śuciśuklavitatapaṭaikadeśacyutamathavā harmyatalaparibhraṣṭamanyairvā
                        śucibhirbhājanairgṛhītaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mṛnmaye vā pātre nidadhyāt | tat
                        sarvakālamupayuñjīta, tasyālābhe bhaumam | taccākāśaguṇabahulam | tat punaḥ
                        saptavidham | tadyathā- kaupaṃ, nādeyaṃ, sārasaṃ, tāḍāgaṃ, prāsravaṇam,
                        audbhidaṃ, cauṇṭyamiti ||7|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8"> tatra varṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhidaṃ vā seveta, mahāguṇatvāt;
                        śaradi sarvaṃ, prasannatvāt; hemante sārasaṃ tāḍāgaṃ vā; vasante kaupaṃ
                        prāsravaṇaṃ vā; grīṣme'pyevaṃ; prāvṛṣi cauṇṭyamanabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ ceti
                        ||8|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9"> kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśavakothapradūṣitam |
                        tṛṇaparṇotkarayutaṃ kaluṣaṃ viṣasaṃyutam ||9|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10"> yo'vagāheta varṣāsu pibed vā'pi navaṃ jalam | sa
                        bāhyābhyantarān rogān prāpnuyāt kṣiprameva tu ||10|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11"> tatra yat
                        paṅkaśaivalahaṭhatṛṇapadmapatraprabhṛtibhiravacchannaṃ
                        raviśaśikiraṇānilairnābhijuṣṭaṃ gandhavarṇarasopasṛṣṭaṃ tadvyāpannamiti
                        vidyāt | tasya sparśarūparasagandhavīryavipākadoṣāḥ ṣaṭ sambhavanti | tatra,
                        kharatā paicchilyamauṣṇyaṃ dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ,
                        paṅkasikatāśaivālabahuvarṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ; vyaktarasatā rasadoṣaḥ;
                        aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ; yadupayuktaṃ
                        tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekānāpādayati sa viryadoṣaḥ; yadupayuktaṃ
                        cirādvipacyate viṣṭambhayati vā sa vipākadoṣa iti | ta ete āntarikṣe na
                        santi ||11|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12"> vyāpannasya cāgnikvathanaṃ sūryātapapratāpanaṃ
                        taptāyaḥpiṇḍasikatāloṣṭrāṇāṃ vā nirvāpaṇaṃ prasādanaṃ ca kartavyaṃ,
                        nāgacampakotpalapāṭalāpuṣpaprabhṛtibhiścādhivāsanamiti ||12|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.13"> sauvarṇe rājate tāmre kāṃsye maṇimaye'pi vā |
                        puṣpāvataṃsaṃ bhaume vā sugandhi salilaṃ pibet ||13|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.14"> vyāpannaṃ varjayennityaṃ toyaṃ yaccāpyanārtavam |
                        doṣasañjananaṃ hyetannādadītāhitaṃ tu tat ||14||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.15"> vyāpannamudakaṃ yastu pibatīhāprasāditam | śvayathuṃ
                        pāṇḍurogaṃ ca tvagdoṣamavipākatām ||15||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.16"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyaśūlagulmodarāṇi ca | anyānvā
                        viṣamānrogānprāpnuyādacireṇa saḥ ||16|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.17"> tatra sapta kaluṣasya prasādanāni bhavanti | tadyathā-
                        katakagomedakabisagranthiśaivālamūlavastrāṇi muktāmaṇiśceti ||17|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.18"> pañca nikṣepaṇāni bhavanti | tadyathā- phalakaṃ,
                        tryaṣṭakaṃ, muñjavalaya, udakamañcikā, śikyaṃ ceti ||18|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.19"> sapta śītīkaraṇāni bhavanti; tadyathā- pravātasthāpanam,
                        udakaprakṣepaṇaṃ, yaṣṭikābhrāmaṇaṃ, vyajanaṃ, vastroddharaṇaṃ,
                        vālukāprakṣepaṇaṃ, śikyāvalambanaṃ ceti ||19|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.20"> nirgandhamavyaktarasaṃ tṛṣṇāghnaṃ śuci śītalam | acchaṃ
                        laghu ca hṛdyaṃ ca toyaṃ guṇavaducyate ||20|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.21"> tatra nadyaḥ paścimābhimukhāḥ pathyāḥ, laghūdakatvāt;
                        pūrvābhimukhāstu na praśasyante, gurūdakatvāt; dakṣiṇābhimukhā nātidoṣalāḥ,
                        sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra sahyaprabhavāḥkuṣṭhaṃ janayanti, vindhyaprabhavāḥ
                        kuṣṭhaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca, malayaprabhavāḥ kṛmīn, mahendraprabhavāḥ
                        ślīpadodarāṇi, himavatprabhavā hṛdrogaśvayathuśirorogaślīpadagalagaṇḍān,
                        prācyāvantyā aparāvantyāścārśāṃsyupajanayanti, pāriyātraprabhavāḥ pathyā
                        balārogyakarya iti ||21|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.22"> nadyaḥ śīghravahā laghvyaḥ proktā yāścāmalodakāḥ |
                        gurvyaḥ śaivālasañchannāḥ kaluṣā mandagāśca yāḥ ||22|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.23"> prāyeṇa nadyo maruṣu satiktā lavaṇānvitāḥ | laghvyaḥ
                        samadhurāścaiva pauruṣeyā bale hitāḥ ||23|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.24"> tatra sarveṣāmeva bhaumānāṃ grahaṇaṃ pratyūṣasi, tatra
                        hyamalatvaṃ śaityaṃ cādhikaṃ bhavati, sa eva cāpāṃ paro guṇa iti ||24|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.25"> divārkakiraṇairjuṣṭaṃ niśāyāminduraśmibhiḥ |
                        arūkṣamanabhiṣyandi tattulyaṃ gaganāmbunā ||25|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.26"> gaganāmbu tridoṣaghnaṃ gṛhītaṃ yat subhājane | balyaṃ
                        rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ pātrāpekṣi tataḥ param ||26|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.27"> rakṣoghnaṃ śītalaṃ hlādi jvaradāhaviṣāpaham |
                        candrakāntodbhavaṃ vāri pittaghnaṃ vimalaṃ smṛtam ||27|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.28"> mūrcchāpittoṣṇadāheṣu viṣe rakte madātyaye |
                        bhramaklamaparīteṣu tamake vamathau tathā ||28| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.29.1"> ūrdhvage raktapitte ca śītamambhaḥ praśasyate |29| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.29.2"> pārśvaśūle pratiśyāye vātaroge galagrahe ||29|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.30"> ādhmāne stimite koṣṭhe sadyaḥśuddhe navajvare | hikkāyāṃ
                        snehapīte ca śītāmbu parivarjayet ||30|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.31"> nādeyaṃ vātalaṃ rūkṣaṃ dīpanaṃ laghu lekhanam |
                        tadabhiṣyandi madhuraṃ sāndraṃ guru kaphāvaham ||31|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.32"> tṛṣṇāghnaṃ sārasaṃ balyaṃ kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ laghu |
                        tāḍāgaṃ vātalaṃ svādu kaṣāyaṃ kaṭupāki ca ||32|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.33"> vātaśleṣmaharaṃ vāpyaṃ sakṣāraṃ kaṭu pittalam | sakṣāraṃ
                        pittalaṃ kaupaṃ śleṣmaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ laghu ||33|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.34"> cauṇṭyamagnikaraṃ rūkṣaṃ madhuraṃ kaphakṛnna ca |
                        kaphaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ laghu prasravaṇodbhavam ||34|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.35"> madhuraṃ pittaśamanamavidāhyaudbhidaṃ smṛtam | vaikiraṃ
                        kaṭu sakṣāraṃ śleṣmaghnaṃ laghu dīpanam ||35|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.36"> kaidāraṃ madhuraṃ proktaṃ vipāke guru doṣalam |
                        tadvatpālvalamuddiṣṭaṃ viśeṣāddoṣalaṃ tu tat ||36|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.37.1"> sāmudramudakaṃ visraṃ lavaṇaṃ sarvadoṣakṛt |37|</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.37.2"> anekadoṣamānūpaṃ vāryabhiṣyandi garhitam ||37|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.38"> ebhirdoṣairasaṃyuktaṃ niravadyaṃ tu jāṅgalam |
                        pāke'vidāhi tṛṣṇāghnaṃ praśastaṃ prītivardhanam ||38|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.39"> dīpanaṃ svādu śītaṃ ca toyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ laghu |39|
                        kaphamedo'nilāmaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ bastiśodhanam ||39|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.40"> śvāsakāsajvaraharaṃ pathyamuṣṇodakaṃ sadā |40| yat
                        kvāthyamānaṃ nirvegaṃ niṣphenaṃ nirmalaṃ laghu ||40||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.41"> caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu tattoyaṃ guṇavat smṛtam |41| na ca
                        paryuṣitaṃ deyaṃ kadācidvāri jānatā ||41|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.42"> amlībhūtaṃ kaphotkledi na hitaṃ tat pipāsave |42|
                        madyapānātsamudbhūte roge pittotthite tathā ||42|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.43"> sannipātasamutthe ca śṛtaśītaṃ praśasyate |43| snigdhaṃ
                        svādu himaṃ hṛdyaṃ dīpanaṃ bastiśodhanam ||43|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.45"> vṛṣyaṃ pittapipāsāghnaṃ nālikerodakaṃ guru |44|
                        dāhātīsārapittāsṛṅmūrcchāmadyaviṣārtiṣu ||44|| śṛtaśītaṃ jalaṃ śastaṃ
                        tṛṣṇācchardibhrameṣu ca |45| arocake pratiśyāye praseke śvayathau kṣaye
                        ||45|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.46"> mande'gnāvudare kuṣṭhe jvare netrāmaye tathā | vraṇe ca
                        madhumehe ca pānīyaṃ mandamācaret ||46|| iti jalavargaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.47"> atha kṣīravargaḥ | gavyamājaṃ tathā cauṣṭramāvikaṃ
                        māhiṣaṃ ca yat | aśvāyāścaiva nāryāśca kareṇūnāṃ ca yatpayaḥ ||47|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.48"> tattvanekauṣadhirasaprasādaṃ prāṇadaṃ guru | madhuraṃ
                        picchilaṃ śītaṃ snigdhaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ saraṃ mṛdu | sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ tasmāt
                        sātmyaṃ kṣīramihocyate ||48|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.49"> tatra sarvameva kṣīraṃ prāṇināmapratiṣiddhaṃ
                        jātisātmyāt, vātapittaśoṇitamānaseṣvapi vikāreṣvaviruddhaṃ,
                        jīrṇajvarakāsaśvāsaśoṣakṣayagulmonmādodaramūrcchābhramamadadāhapipāsāhṛdbastidoṣa-
                        pāṇḍurogagrahaṇīdoṣārśaḥśūlodāvartātisārapravāhikāyonirogagarbhāsrāvaraktapittaśramaklamaharaṃ,
                        pāpmāpahaṃ balyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ vājīkaraṇaṃ rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ vayaḥsthāpanamāyuṣyaṃ
                        jīvanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ sandhānaṃ vamanavirecanāsthāpanaṃ tulyaguṇatvāccaujaso
                        vardhanaṃ bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇānāṃ kṣudvyavāyavyāyāmakarśitānāṃ ca
                        pathyatamam ||49|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.50"> alpābhiṣyandi gokṣīraṃ snigdhaṃ guru rasāyanam |
                        raktapittaharaṃ śītaṃ madhuraṃ rasapākayoḥ ||50|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.51"> jīvanīyaṃ tathā vātapittaghnaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam |51|
                        gavyatulyaguṇaṃ tvājaṃ viśeṣācchoṣiṇāṃ hitam ||51|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.52"> dīpanaṃ laghu saṅgrāhi śvāsakāsāsrapittanut |
                        ajānāmalpakāyatvāt kaṭutiktaniṣevaṇāt ||52|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.53">nātyambupānādvyāyāmāt sarvavyādhiharaṃ payaḥ |53|
                        rūkṣoṣṇaṃ lavaṇaṃ kiñcidauṣṭraṃ svādurasaṃ laghu ||53|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.54">śophagulmodarārśoghnaṃ kṛmikuṣṭhaviṣāpaham |54| āvikaṃ
                        madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ guru pittakaphāvaham ||54|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.55.1"> pathyaṃ kevalavāteṣu kāse cānilasambhave |55| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.55.2"> mahābhiṣyandi madhuraṃ māhiṣaṃ vahnināśanam ||55|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.56"> nidrākaraṃ śītataraṃ gavyāt snigdhataraṃ guru |56|
                        uṣṇamaikaśaphaṃ balyaṃ śākhāvātaharaṃ payaḥ ||56|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.57"> madhurāmlarasaṃ rūkṣaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ laghu |57| nāryāstu
                        madhuraṃ stanyaṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ himam ||57|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.58"> nasyāścyotanayoḥ pathyaṃ jīvanaṃ laghu dīpanam |58|
                        hastinyā madhuraṃ vṛṣyaṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ guru ||58|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.59">snigdhaṃ sthairyakaraṃ śītaṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ balavardhanam |59|
                        prāyaḥ prābhātikaṃ kṣīraṃ guru viṣṭambhi śītalam ||59|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.60"> rātryāḥ somaguṇatvācca vyāyāmābhāvatastathā |60|
                        divākarābhitaptānāṃ vyāyāmānilasevanāt ||60|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.61"> śramaghnaṃ vātanuccaiva cakṣuṣyaṃ cāparāhṇikam |61|
                        payo'bhiṣyandi gurvāmaṃ prāyaśaḥ parikīrtitam ||61|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.62"> tadevoktaṃ laghutaramanabhiṣyandi vai śṛtam |62|
                        varjayitvā striyāḥ stanyamāmameva hi taddhitam ||62|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.63"> dhāroṣṇaṃ guṇavat kṣīraṃ viparītamato'nyathā |63|
                        tadevātiśṛtaṃ śītaṃ guru bṛṃhaṇamucyate ||63|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.64"> aniṣṭagandhamamlaṃ ca vivarṇaṃ virasaṃ ca yat | varjyaṃ
                        salavaṇaṃ kṣīraṃ yacca vigrathitaṃ bhavet ||64|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.65"> iti kṣīravargaḥ | atha dadhivargaḥ | dadhi tu
                        madhuramamlamatyamlaṃ ceti; tatkaṣāyānurasaṃ snigdhamuṣṇaṃ
                        pīnasaviṣamajvarātisārārocakamūtrakṛcchrakārśyāpahaṃ vṛṣyaṃ prāṇakaraṃ
                        maṅgalyaṃ ca ||65|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.66"> mahābhiṣyandi madhuraṃ kaphamedovivardhanam |
                        kaphapittakṛdamlaṃ syādatyamlaṃ raktadūṣaṇam ||66|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.67"> vidāhi sṛṣṭaviṇmūtraṃ mandajātaṃ tridoṣakṛt |67|
                        snigdhaṃ vipāke madhuraṃ dīpanaṃ balavardhanam ||67|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.68"> vātāpahaṃ pavitraṃ ca dadhi gavyaṃ rucipradam |68|
                        dadhyājaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ laghu vātakṣayāpaham ||68|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.69"> durnāmaśvāsakāseṣu hitamagneśca dīpanam |69| vipāke
                        madhuraṃ vṛṣyaṃ vātapittaprasādanam ||69|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.70">balāsavardhanaṃ snigdhaṃ viśeṣāddadhi māhiṣam |70| vipāke
                        kaṭu sakṣāraṃ guru bhedyauṣṭrikaṃ dadhi ||70|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.71">vātamarśāṃsi kuṣṭhāni kṛmīn hantyudarāṇi ca |71| kopanaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.72"> rase pāke ca madhuramatyabhiṣyandi doṣalam |72|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.73"> rūkṣamuṣṇaṃ kaṣāyaṃ ca kaphamūtrāpahaṃ ca tat |73|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.82">amlaṃ kaṣāyaṃ madhuramavṛṣyaṃ kaphavātanut | prahlādanaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.92"> navanītaṃ punaḥ sadyaskaṃ laghu sukumāraṃ madhuraṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.96">iti takravargaḥ | atha ghṛtam | ghṛtaṃ tu madhuraṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.112"> iti ghṛtavargaḥ | atha tailāni | tailaṃ tvāgneyamuṣṇaṃ

                        medhāmārdavamāṃsasthairyavarṇabalakaraṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ baddhamūtraṃ lekhanaṃ
                        tiktakaṣāyānurasaṃ pācanamanilabalāsakṣayakaraṃ krimighnamaśitapittajananaṃ

                        chinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭacyutamathitakṣatapiccitabhagnasphuṭitakṣārāgnidagdhaviśliṣṭadāritā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.115">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.131"> grāmyānūpaudakānāṃ ca vasāmedomajjāno gurūṣṇamadhurā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.132"> atha madhuvargaḥ | madhu tu madhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ

                        pittaśleṣmamedomehahikkāśvāsakāsātisāraccharditṛṣṇākṛmiviṣapraśamanaṃ hlādi
                        tridoṣapraśamanaṃ ca; tattu laghutvāt kaphaghnaṃ, paicchilyānmādhuryāt

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.135">paicchilyāt svādubhūyastvādbhrāmaraṃ gurusañjñitam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.143"> tattu nānādravyarasaguṇavīryavipākaviruddhānāṃ
                        puṣparasānāṃ makṣikāsambhavatvāccānuṣṇopacāram ||143|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.144"> uṣṇairvirudhyate sarvaṃ viṣānvayatayā madhu |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.145"> tatsaukumāryācca tathaiva śaityānnānauṣadhīnāṃ
                        rasasambhavācca | uṣṇairvirudhyeta viśeṣataśca tathā'ntarīkṣeṇa jalena cāpi

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.146"> uṣṇena madhu saṃyuktaṃ vamaneṣvavacāritam |
                        apākādanavasthānānna virudhyeta pūrvavat ||146|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.147"> madhvāmātparatastvanyadāmaṃ kaṣṭaṃ na vidyate |
                        viruddhopakramatvāttat sarvaṃ hanti yathā viṣam ||147|| iti madhuvargaḥ
                        |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.148"> athekṣuvargaḥ | ikṣavo madhurā madhuravipākā guravaḥ
                        śītāḥ snigdhā balyā vṛṣyā mūtralā raktapittapraśamanāḥ kṛmikaphakarāśceti |
                        te cānekavidhāḥ | tadyathā- ||148|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.149">pauṇḍrako bhīrukaścaiva vaṃśakaḥ śvetaporakaḥ |
                        kāntārastāpasekṣuśca kāṣṭhekṣuḥ sūcipatrakaḥ ||149|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.150"> naipālo dīrghapatraśca nīlaporo'tha kośakṛt | ityetā
                        jātayaḥ sthaulyād, ... |150|... guṇān vakṣyāmyataḥ param ||150|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.151"> suśīto madhuraḥ snigdho bṛṃhaṇaḥ śleṣmalaḥ saraḥ |
                        avidāhī gururvṛṣyaḥ pauṇḍrako bhīrukastathā ||151|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.152">ābhyāṃ tulyaguṇaḥ kiñcitsakṣāro vaṃśako mataḥ |
                        vaṃśavacchvetaporastu kiñciduṣṇaḥ sa vātahā ||152|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.153"> kāntāratāpasāvikṣū vaṃśakānugatau matau | evaṅguṇastu
                        kāṣṭhekṣuḥ sa tu vātaprakopaṇaḥ ||153|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.154"> sūcīpatro nīlaporau naipālo dīrghapatrakaḥ | vātalāḥ
                        kaphapittaghnāḥ sakaṣāyā vidāhinaḥ ||154|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.155"> kośakāro guruḥ śīto raktapittakṣayāpahaḥ |155| atīva
                        madhuro mūle madhye madhura eva tu ||155||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.156"> agreṣvakṣiṣu vijñeya ikṣūṇāṃ lavaṇo rasaḥ ||156|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.157"> avidāhī kaphakaro vātapittanivāraṇaḥ | vaktraprahlādano
                        vṛṣyo dantaniṣpīḍito rasaḥ ||157|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.158"> gururvidāhī viṣṭambhī yāntrikastu prakīrtitaḥ |158|
                        pakvo guruḥ saraḥ snigdhaḥ satīkṣṇaḥ kaphavātanut ||158|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.159"> phāṇitaṃ guru madhuramabhiṣyandi bṛṃhaṇamavṛṣyaṃ
                        tridoṣakṛcca ||159|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.160"> guḍaḥ sakṣāramadhuro nātiśītaḥ snigdho
                        mūtraraktaśodhano nātipittajidvātaghno medaḥkṛmikaphakaro balyo vṛṣyaśca
                        ||160|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.161"> pittaghno madhuraḥ śuddho vātaghno'sṛkprasādanaḥ |161|
                        sapurāṇo'dhikaguṇo guḍaḥ pathyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||161|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.162"> matsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarā vimalajātā uttarottaraṃ śītāḥ
                        snigdhāḥ gurutarā madhuratarā vṛṣyā raktapittapraśamanāstṛṣṇāpraśamanāśca
                        ||162|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.163"> yathā yathaiṣāṃ vaimalyaṃ madhuratvaṃ tathā tathā |
                        snehagauravaśaityāni saratvaṃ ca tathā tathā ||163|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.164"> yo yo matsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarāṇāṃ svako guṇaḥ | tena
                        tenaiva nirdeśyasteṣāṃ visrāvaṇo guṇaḥ ||164|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.165"> sārasthitā suvimalā niḥkṣārā ca yathā yathā | tathā
                        guṇavatī sarvā vijñeyā śarkarā budhaiḥ ||165|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.166"> madhuśarkarā punaśchardyatīsāraharī rūkṣā chedanī
                        prasādanī kaṣāyamadhurā madhuravipākā ca ||166|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.167"> yavāsaśarkarā madhurakaṣāyā tiktānurasā śleṣmaharī sarā
                        ceti ||167|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.168"> yāvatyaḥ śarkarāḥ proktāḥ sarvā dāhapraṇāśanāḥ |
                        raktapittapraśamanāśchardimūrcchātṛṣāpahāḥ ||168|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.169"> rūkṣaṃ madhūkapuṣpotthaṃ phāṇitaṃ vātapittakṛt |
                        kaphaghnaṃ madhuraṃ pāke kaṣāyaṃ bastidūṣaṇam ||169|| itīkṣuvargaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.170"> atha madyavargaḥ | sarvaṃ pittakaraṃ madyamamlaṃ
                        rocanadīpanam | bhedanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ hṛdyaṃ bastiviśodhanam ||170|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.171"> pāke laghu vidāhyuṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇamindriyabodhanam | vikāsi
                        sṛṣṭaviṇmūtraṃ... |171| ... śṛṇu tasya viśeṣaṇam ||171|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.172"> mārdvīkamavidāhitvānmadhurānvayatastathā |
                        raktapitte'pi satataṃ budhairna pratiṣidhyate ||172|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.173"> madhuraṃ taddhi rūkṣaṃ ca kaṣāyānurasaṃ laghu |
                        laghupāki saraṃ śoṣaviṣamajvaranāśanam ||173||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.174"> mārdvīkālpāntaraṃ kiñcit khārjūraṃ vātakopanam | tadeva
                        viśadaṃ rucyaṃ kaphaghnaṃ karśanaṃ laghu ||174|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.175"> kaṣāyamadhuraṃ hṛdyaṃ sugandhīndriyabodhanam |175|
                        kāsārśograhaṇīdoṣamūtrāghātānilāpahā ||175|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.176"> stanyaraktakṣayahitā surā bṛṃhaṇadīpanī |176|
                        kāsārśograhaṇīśvāsapratiśyāyavināśanī ||176|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.177"> śvetā mūtrakaphastanyaraktamāṃsakarī surā |177|
                        chardyarocakahṛtkukṣitodaśūlapramardanī ||177|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.178">prasannā kaphavātārśovibandhānāhanāśanī |178|

                        ||179|| ... śleṣmalaṃ tu madhūlakam ||178|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.179"> rūkṣā nātikaphā vṛṣyā pācanī cākṣikī smṛtā ||179|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.180"> tridoṣo bhedyavṛṣyaśca kohalo vadanapriyaḥ |180|
                        grāhyuṣṇo jagalaḥ paktā rūkṣastṛṭkaphaśophakṛt ||180|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.181">hṛdyaḥ pravāhikāṭopadurnāmānilaśoṣahṛt |181| bakkaso
                        hṛtasāratvādviṣṭambhī vātakopanaḥ ||181|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.182"> dīpanaḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtro viśado'lpamado guruḥ |182| kaṣāyo
                        madhuraḥ śīdhurgauḍaḥ pācanadīpanaḥ ||182|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.183"> śārkaro madhuro rucyo dīpano bastiśodhanaḥ | vātaghno
                        madhuraḥ pāke hṛdya indriyabodhanaḥ ||183|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.184"> tadvat pakvarasaḥ śīdhurbalavarṇakaraḥ saraḥ |
                        śophaghno dīpano hṛdyo rucyaḥ śleṣmārśasāṃ hitaḥ ||184|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.185"> karśanaḥ śītarasikaḥ śvayathūdaranāśanaḥ |
                        varṇakṛjjaraṇaḥ svaryo vibandhaghno'rśasāṃ hitaḥ ||185|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.186"> ākṣikaḥ pāṇḍurogaghno vraṇyaḥ saṅgrāhako laghuḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.187"> jāmbavo baddhanisyandastuvaro vātakopanaḥ |187| tīkṣṇaḥ
                        surāsavo hṛdyo mūtralaḥ kaphavātanut ||187|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.188"> mukhapriyaḥ sthiramado vijñeyo'nilanāśanaḥ |188|
                        laghurmadhvāsavaśchedī mehakuṣṭhaviṣāpahaḥ ||188|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.189">tiktaḥ kaṣāyaḥ śophaghnastīkṣṇaḥ svāduravātakṛt |189|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.190"> kṛmimedonilaharo maireyo madhuro guruḥ |190| balyaḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.191"> śīdhurmadhūkapuṣpottho vihāhyagnibalapradaḥ | rūkṣaḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.192"> nirdiśedrasataścānyān kandamūlaphalāsavān |192| navaṃ
                        madyamabhiṣyandi guru vātādikopanam ||192|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.193"> aniṣṭagandhi virasamahṛdyaṃ ca vidāhi ca |193| sugandhi
                        dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ rociṣṇu kṛmināśanam ||193|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.194"> sphuṭasrotaskaraṃ jīrṇaṃ laghu vātakaphāpaham |194|
                        ariṣṭo dravyasaṃyogasaṃskārādadhiko guṇaiḥ ||194|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.195"> bahudoṣaharaścaiva doṣāṇāṃ śamanaśca saḥ | dīpanaḥ
                        kaphavātaghnaḥ saraḥ pittāvirodhanaḥ ||195|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.196"> śūlādhmānodaraplīhajvarājīrṇārśasāṃ hitaḥ |196|
                        pippalyādikṛto gulmakapharogaharaḥ smṛtaḥ ||196|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.197"> cikitsiteṣu vakṣyante'riṣṭā rogaharāḥ pṛthak |197|
                        ariṣṭāsavaśīdhūnāṃ guṇān karmāṇi cādiśet ||197|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.198"> buddhyā yathāsvaṃ saṃskāramavekṣya kuśalo bhiṣak |198|
                        sāndraṃ vidāhi durgandhaṃ virasaṃ kṛmilaṃ guru ||198|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.199"> ahṛdyaṃ taruṇaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ durbhājanasthitam |
                        alpauṣadhaṃ paryuṣitamatyacchaṃ picchilaṃ ca yat ||199||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.200"> tadvarjyaṃ sarvathā madyaṃ kiñciccheṣaṃ tu yadbhavet |
                        tatra yat stokasambhāraṃ taruṇaṃ picchilaṃ guru ||200||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.201"> kaphaprakopi tanmadyaṃ durjaraṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
                        pittaprakopi bahalaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ vidāhi ca ||201|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.202">ahṛdyaṃ pelavaṃ pūti kṛmilaṃ virasaṃ ca yat | tathā
                        paryuṣitaṃ cāpi vidyādanilakopanam ||202||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.203">sarvadoṣairupetaṃ tu sarvadoṣaprakopaṇam |203|
                        cirasthitaṃ jātarasaṃ dīpanaṃ kaphavātajit ||203|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.204">rucyaṃ prasannaṃ surabhi madyaṃ sevyaṃ madāvaham |204|
                        tasyānekaprakārasya madyasya rasavīryataḥ ||204|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.205"> saukṣmyādauṣṇyācca taikṣṇyācca vikāsitvācca vahninā
                        sametya hṛdayaṃ prāpya dhamanīrūrdhvamāgatam | vicālyendriyacetāṃsi vīryaṃ
                        madayate'cirāt ||205||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.206"> cireṇa ślaiṣmike puṃsi pānato jāyate madaḥ |
                        acirādvātike dṛṣṭaḥ, paittike śīghrameva ca ||206|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.207"> sāttvike śaucadākṣiṇyaharṣamaṇḍanalālasaḥ |
                        gītādhyayanasaubhāgyasuratotsāhakṛnmadaḥ ||207|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.208">rājase duḥkhaśīlatvamātmatyāgaṃ sasāhasam | kalahaṃ
                        sānubandhaṃ tu karoti puruṣe madaḥ ||208|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.209"> aśaucanidrāmātsaryāgamyāgamanalolatāḥ | asatyabhāṣaṇaṃ
                        cāpi kuryāddhi tāmase madaḥ ||209|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.210"> raktapittakaraṃ śuktaṃ chedanaṃ bhuktapācanam |
                        vaisvaryaṃ jaraṇaṃ śleṣmapāṇḍukrimiharaṃ laghu ||210|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.211">tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ mūtralaṃ hṛdyaṃ kaphaghnaṃ kaṭupāki ca |211|
                        tadvattadāsutaṃ sarvaṃ rocanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||211|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.212"> gauḍāni rasaśuktāni madhuśuktāni yāni ca | yathāpūrvaṃ
                        gurutarāṇyabhiṣyandakarāṇi ca ||212|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.213"> tuṣāmbu dīpanaṃ hṛdyaṃ hṛtpāṇḍukṛmiroganut |
                        grahaṇyarśovikāraghnaṃ bhedi sauvīrakaṃ tathā ||213|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.214"> dhānyāmlaṃ dhānyayonitvājjīvanaṃ dāhanāśanam | sparśāt
                        pānāttu pavanakaphatṛṣṇāharaṃ laghu ||214|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.215"> taikṣṇyācca nirharedāśu kaphaṃ gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇāt |
                        mukhavairasyadaurgandhyamalaśoṣaklamāpaham ||215|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.216">dīpanaṃ jaraṇaṃ bhedi hitamāsthāpaneṣu ca |
                        samudramāśritānāṃ ca janānāṃ sātmyamucyate ||216|| iti madhyavargaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.217"> atha mūtrāṇi | mūtrāṇi
                        gomahiṣyajāvigajahayakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ tīkṣṇānyuṣṇāni kaṭūni tiktāni
                        lavaṇānurasāni laghūni śodhanāni
                        kaphavātakṛmimedoviṣagulmārśadarakuṣṭhaśophārocakapāṇḍurogaharāṇi hṛdyāni
                        dīpanāni ca sāmānyataḥ ||217|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.218">bhavataścātra- tat sarvaṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ
                        laghu | śodhanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ kṛmimedoviṣāpaham ||218|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.219"> arśojaṭharagulmaghnaṃ śophārocakanāśanam |
                        pāṇḍurogaharaṃ bhedi hṛdyaṃ dīpanapācanam ||219|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.220"> gomūtraṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ sakṣāratvānna vātalam |
                        laghvagnidīpanaṃ medhyaṃ pittalaṃ kaphavātanut ||220|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.221"> śūlagulmodarānāhavirekāsthāpanādiṣu |
                        mūtraprayogasādhyeṣu gavyaṃ mūtraṃ prayojayet ||221|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.222"> durnāmodaraśūleṣu kuṣṭhamehāviśuddhiṣu |
                        ānāhaśophagulmeṣu pāṇḍuroge ca māhiṣam ||222|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.223"> kāsaśvāsāpahaṃ śophakāmalāpāṇḍuroganut |
                        kaṭutiktānvitaṃ chāgamīṣanmārutakopanam ||223|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.224"> kāsaplīhodaraśvāsaśoṣavarcograhe hitam | sakṣāraṃ
                        tiktakaṭukamuṣṇaṃ vātaghnamāvikam ||224|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.225"> dīpanaṃ kaṭu tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ vātacetovikāranut | āśvaṃ
                        kaphaharaṃ mūtraṃ kṛmidadruṣu śasyate ||225|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.226"> satiktaṃ lavaṇaṃ bhedi vātaghnaṃ pittakopanam | tīkṣṇaṃ
                        kṣāre kilāse ca nāgaṃ mūtraṃ prayojayet ||226|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.227"> garacetovikāraghnaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ grahaṇiroganut | dīpanaṃ
                        gārdabhaṃ mūtraṃ kṛmivātakaphāpaham ||227|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.228"> śophakuṣṭhodaronmādamārutakrimināśanam | arśoghnaṃ
                        kārabhaṃ mūtraṃ... |228| ... mānuṣaṃ ca viṣāpaham ||228|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.229"> dravadravyāṇi sarvāṇi samāsāt kīrtitāni tu |
                        kāladeśavibhāgajño nṛpaterdātumarhati ||229|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        dravadravyavijñānīyo nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ||45|| </l>
                </div>
                <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3"> dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca- prāgabhihitaḥ
                        ‘prāṇināṃ punarmūlamāhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca, sa ṣaṭsu raseṣvāyattaḥ, rasāḥ
                        punardravyāśrayiṇaḥ,’ dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī
                        doṣāṇāṃ sāmyaṃ ca, brahmāderapi ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthityutpattivināśahetuḥ,
                        āhārādevābhivṛddhirbalamārogyaṃ varṇendriyaprasādaśca, tathā
                        hyāhāravaiṣamyādasvāsthyaṃ; tasyāśitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpasyānekavidhaprabhāvasya pṛthak
                        pṛthagdravyarasaguṇavīryavipākakarmāṇīcchāmi jñātuṃ, na
                        hyanavabuddhasvabhāvā bhiṣajaḥ svasthānuvṛttiṃ roganigrahaṇaṃ ca kartuṃ
                        samarthāḥ; āhārāyattāśca sarvaprāṇino yasmāttasmādannapānavidhimupadiśatu me
                        bhagavānityuktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ- atha khalu vatsa suśruta!
                        yathāpraśnamucyamānamupadhārayasva- ||3|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4"> tatra,
                        lohitaśālikalamakardamakapāṇḍukasugandhakaśakunāhṛtapuṣpāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukarodhrapuṣpaka-
                        dīrghaśūkakāñcanakamahiṣamahāśūkahāyanakadūṣakamahādūṣakaprabhṛtayaḥ śālayaḥ
                        ||4|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5"> madhurā vīryataḥ śītā laghupākā balāvahāḥ |
                        pittaghnālpānilakaphāḥ snigdhā baddhālpavarcasaḥ ||5|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6"> teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ |
                        cakṣuṣyo varṇabalakṛt svaryo hṛdyastṛṣāpahaḥ ||6|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7"> vraṇyo jvaraharaścaiva sarvadoṣaviṣāpahaḥ |7|
                        tasmādalpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo'varāḥ ||7|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8">
                        ṣaṣṭikakāṅgukamukundakapītakapramodakakākalakāsanapuṣpakamahāṣaṣṭikacūrṇakakuravakakedāraprabhṛtayaḥ
                        ṣaṣṭikāḥ ||8|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9"> rase pāke ca madhurāḥ śamanā vātapittayoḥ | śālīnāṃ ca
                        guṇaistulyā bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphaśukralāḥ ||9|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10"> ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravarasteṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | mṛduḥ
                        snigdhastridoṣaghnaḥ sthairyakṛdbalavardhanaḥ ||10|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11"> vipāke madhuro grāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ |11|
                        śeṣāstvalpāntarāstasmāt ṣaṣṭikāḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ ||11|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12">
                        kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhajatumukhanandīmukhalāvākṣakatvaritakakukkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalaprabhṛtayo
                        vrīhayaḥ ||12|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke'madhurā vīryato'himāḥ |
                        alpābhiṣyandinastulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikairbaddhavarcasaḥ ||13|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14"> kṛṣṇavrīhirvarasteṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
                        tasmādalpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśo vrīhayo'pare ||14|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15"> dagdhāyāmavanau jātāḥ śālayo laghupākinaḥ | kaṣāyā
                        baddhaviṇmūtrā rūkṣāḥ śleṣmāpakarṣaṇāḥ ||15|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.16"> sthalajāḥ kaphapittaghnāḥ kaṣāyāḥ kaṭukānvayāḥ |
                        kiñcitsatiktamadhurāḥ pavanānalavardhanāḥ ||16|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.17"> kaidārā madhurā vṛṣyā balyāḥ pittanibarhaṇāḥ |
                        īṣatkaṣāyālpamalā guravaḥ kaphaśukralāḥ ||17|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.18"> ropyātiropyā laghavaḥ śīghrapākā guṇottarāḥ | adāhino
                        doṣaharā balyā mūtravivardhanāḥ ||18|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.19"> śālayaśchinnarūḍhā ye rūkṣāste baddhavarcasaḥ | tiktāḥ
                        kaṣāyāḥ pittaghnā laghupākāḥ kaphāpahāḥ ||19|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.20"> vistareṇāyamuddiṣṭaḥ śālivargo hitāhitaḥ |20| iti
                        śālivargaḥ | atha kudhānyavargaḥ | tadvat kudhānyamudgādimāṣādīnāṃ ca
                        vakṣyate ||20|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.21">
                        koradūṣakaśyāmākanīvāraśāntanuvarakoddālakapriyaṅgumadhūlikānandīmukhī-
                        kuruvindagavedhukasarabarukatoda(ya)parṇīmukundakaveṇuyavaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        kudhānyaviśeṣāḥ ||21|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.22"> uṣṇāḥ kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ | śleṣmaghnā
                        baddhanisyandā vātapittaprakopaṇāḥ ||22|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.23"> kaṣāyamadhurasteṣāṃ śītaḥ pittāpahaḥ smṛtaḥ | kodravaśca
                        sanīvāraḥ śyāmākaśca saśāntanuḥ ||23|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.24"> kṛṣṇā raktāśca pītāśca śvetāścaiva priyaṅgavaḥ |
                        yathottaraṃ pradhānāḥ syū rūkṣāḥ kaphaharāḥ smṛtāḥ ||24|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.25"> madhūlī madhurā śītā snigdhā nandīmukhī tathā |25|
                        viśoṣī tatra bhūyiṣṭhaṃ varukaḥ samukundakaḥ ||25|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.26"> rūkṣā veṇuyavā jñeyā vīryoṣṇā kaṭupākinaḥ | baddhamūtrāḥ
                        kaphaharāḥ kaṣāyā vātakopanāḥ ||26|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.27">
                        mudgavanamudgakalāyamakuṣṭhamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakasatīnatripuṭakahareṇvāḍhakīprabhṛtayo
                        vaidalāḥ ||27|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.28"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītāḥ kaṭupākā marutkarāḥ |
                        baddhamūtrapurīṣāśca pittaśleṣmaharāstathā ||28|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.29"> nātyarthaṃ vātalāsteṣu mudgā dṛṣṭiprasādanāḥ | pradhānā
                        haritāstatra vanyā mudgasamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||29|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.30"> vipāke madhurāḥ proktā masūrā baddhavarcasaḥ |30|
                        makuṣṭhakāḥ kṛmikarāḥ... |30| ... kalāyāḥ pracurānilāḥ ||30|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.31"> āḍhakī kaphapittaghnī nātivātaprakopaṇī |31| vātalāḥ
                        śītamadhurāḥ sakaṣāyā virūkṣaṇāḥ ||31|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.32">kaphaśoṇitapittaghnāścaṇakāḥ puṃstvanāśanāḥ | ta eva
                        ghṛtasaṃyuktāstridoṣaśamanāḥ param ||32|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.33"> hareṇavaḥ satīnāśca vijñeyā baddhavarcasaḥ |33| ṛte
                        mudgamasūrābhyāmanye tvādhmānakārakāḥ ||33|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34"> māṣo gururbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdhoṣṇavṛṣyo
                        madhuro'nilaghnaḥ | santarpaṇaḥ stanyakaro viśeṣādbalapradaḥ
                        śukrakaphāvahaśca ||34|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35"> kaṣāyabhāvānna purīṣabhedī na mūtralo naiva kaphasya
                        kartā | svādurvipāke madhuro'lasāndraḥ santarpaṇaḥ stanyarucipradaśca ||35|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36"> māṣaiḥ samānaṃ phalamātmaguptamuktaṃ ca kākāṇḍaphalaṃ
                        tathaiva |36| āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaśca ||36|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37"> uṣṇaḥ kulattho rasataḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭurvipāke
                        kaphamārutaghnaḥ | śukrāśmarīgulmaniṣūdanaśca sāṅgrāhikaḥ pīnasakāsahantā
                        ||37|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38"> ānāhamedogudakīlahikkāśvāsāpahaḥ śoṇitapittakṛcca |
                        kaphasya hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ ||38|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39"> īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ satiktaḥ sāṅgrāhikaḥ
                        pittakarastathoṣṇaḥ | tilo vipāke madhuro baliṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇe lepana eva
                        pathyaḥ ||39|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40"> dantyo'gnimedhājanano'lpamūtrastvacyo'tha keśyo'nilahā
                        guruśca |40| tileṣu sarveṣvasitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarāstathā'nye
                        ||40|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41"> yavaḥ kaṣāyo madhuro himaśca kaṭurvipāke kaphapittahārī
                        | vraṇeṣu pathyastilavacca nityaṃ prabaddhamūtro bahuvātavarcāḥ ||41|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42">sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇakṛcca sapicchilaḥ
                        sthūlavilekhanaśca | medomaruttṛḍ.hharaṇo'tirūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ
                        śoṇitapittayośca ||42|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43"> ebhirguṇairhīnataraistu
                        kiñcidvidyādyavebhyo'tiyavānaśeṣaiḥ |43| godhūma ukto madhuro guruśca balyaḥ
                        sthiraḥ śukrarucipradaśca ||43|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44">snigdho'tiśīto'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛcchleṣmakaraḥ
                        saraśca |44| rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśoṣaśukrabalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī ||44|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45"> kaṭurvipāke madhurastu śimbaḥ
                        prabhinnaviṇmārutapittalaśca |45| sitāsitāḥ pītakaraktavarṇā bhavanti
                        ye'nekavidhāstu śimbāḥ ||45|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46"> yathāditaste guṇataḥ pradhānā jñeyāḥ kaṭūṣṇā
                        rasapākayośca |46| sahādvayaṃ mūlakajāśca śimbāḥ kuśimbivallīprabhavāstu
                        śimbāḥ ||46|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47"> jñeyā vipāke madhurā rase ca balapradāḥ
                        pittanibarhaṇāśca |47| vidāhavantaśca bhṛśaṃ virūkṣā viṣṭabhya
                        jīryantyanilapradāśca ||47|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48"> rucipradāścaiva sudurjarāśca sarve smṛtā vaidalikāstu
                        śimbāḥ |48| kaṭurvipāke kaṭukaḥ kaphaghno vidāhibhāvādahitaḥ kusumbhaḥ
                        ||48|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49"> uṣṇā'tasī svādurasā'nilaghnī pittolbaṇā syāt kaṭukā
                        vipāke | pāke rase cāpi kaṭuḥ pradiṣṭaḥ siddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī
                        ||49||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.50">tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣaḥ
                        kaphamārutaghnastathāguṇaścāsitasarṣapo'pi |50| anārtavaṃ
                        vyādhihatamaparyāgatameva ca | abhūmijaṃ navaṃ cāpi na dhānyaṃ guṇavat
                        smṛtam ||50|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.51"> navaṃ dhānyamabhiṣyandi laghu saṃvatsaroṣitam |51|
                        vidāhi guru viṣṭambhi virūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭidūṣaṇam ||51|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52"> śālyādeḥ sarṣapāntasya vividhasyāsya bhāgaśaḥ |
                        kālapramāṇasaṃskāramātrāḥ samparikīrtitāḥ ||52|| iti kudhānyavargaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53"> atha māṃsavargaḥ | ata ūrdhvaṃ māṃsavargānupadekṣyāmaḥ;
                        tadyathā- jaleśayā, ānūpā, grāmyāḥ, kravyabhuja, ekaśaphā, jāṅgalāśceti
                        ṣaṇmāṃsavargā bhavanti | eteṣāṃ vargāṇāmuttarottarā pradhānatamāḥ | te
                        punardvividhā jāṅgalā ānūpāśceti | tatra jāṅgalavargo'ṣṭavidhaḥ | tadyathā-
                        jaṅghālā, viṣkirāḥ, pratudā, guhāśayāḥ, prasahāḥ, parṇamṛgā, bileśayā,
                        grāmyāśceti | teṣāṃ jaṅghālaviṣkirau pradhānatamau ||53|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54">
                        tāveṇahariṇarkṣakuraṅgakarālakṛtamālaśarabhaśvadaṃṣṭrāpṛṣatacāruṣkaramṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayo
                        jaṅghālā mṛgāḥ kaṣāyā madhurā laghavo vātapittaharāstīkṣṇā hṛdyā
                        bastiśodhanāśca ||54|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55"> kaṣāyamadhuro hṛdyaḥ pittāsṛkkapharogahā | saṅgrāhī
                        rocano balyasteṣāmeṇo jvarāpahaḥ ||55|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56"> madhuro madhuraḥ pāke doṣaghno'naladīpanaḥ | śītalo
                        baddhaviṇmūtra sugandhirhariṇo laghuḥ ||56|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.57"> eṇaḥ kṛṣṇastayorjñeyo hariṇastāmra ucyate | yo na kṛṣṇo
                        na tāmraśca kuraṅgaḥ so'bhidhīyate ||57|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.58"> śītā'sṛkpittaśamanī vijñeyā mṛgamātṛkā |
                        sannipātakṣayaśvāsakāsahikkārucipraṇut ||58|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.59">
                        lāvatittirikapiñjalavartīravartikāvartakanaptṛkāvārtīkacakorakalaviṅkamayūrakrakaropacakra-
                        kukkuṭasāraṅgaśatapatrakutittirikuruvāhakayavālakaprabhṛtayastryāhalā
                        viṣkirāḥ ||59|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60"> laghavaḥ śītamadhurāḥ kaṣāyā doṣanāśanāḥ |60| saṅgrāhī
                        dīpanaścaiva kaṣāyamadhuro laghuḥ | lāvaḥ kaṭuvipākaśca sannipāte tu pūjitaḥ
                        ||60|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.61"> īṣadgurūṣṇamadhuro vṛṣyo medhāgnivardhanaḥ | tittiriḥ
                        sarvadoṣaghno grāhī varṇaprasādanaḥ ||61|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.62"> raktapittaharaḥ śīto laghuścāpi kapiñjalaḥ | kaphottheṣu
                        ca rogeṣu mandavāte ca śasyate ||62||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.63"> hikkāśvāsānilaharo viśeṣādgauratittiriḥ |63|
                        vātapittaharā vṛṣyā medhāgnibalavardhanāḥ ||63|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.64"> laghavaḥ krakarā hṛdyāstathā caivopacakrakāḥ |64|
                        kaṣāyaḥ svādulavaṇastvacyaḥ keśyo'rucau hitaḥ ||64|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.65">mayūraḥ svaramedhāgnidṛkśrotrendriyadārḍhyakṛt |65|
                        snigdhoṣṇo'nilahā vṛṣyaḥ svedasvarabalāvahaḥ ||65|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.66">bṛṃhaṇaḥ kukkuṭo vanyastadvadgrāmyo gurustu saḥ |
                        vātarogakṣayavamīviṣamajvaranāśanaḥ ||66|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.67">
                        kapotapārāvatabhṛṅgarājaparabhṛtakoyaṣṭikakuliṅgagṛhakuliṅgagokṣveḍakaḍiṇḍimāṇavakaśatapatraka-
                        mātṛnindakabhedāśiśukasārikāvalgulīgiriśālaṭvālaṭṭūṣakasugṛhākhañjarīṭahārītadātyūhaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        , pratudāḥ ||67|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.68"> kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ phalāhārā marutkarāḥ |
                        pittaśleṣmaharāḥ śītā baddhamūtrālpavarcasaḥ ||68|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.69"> sarvadoṣakarasteṣāṃ bhedāśī maladūṣakaḥ |69|
                        kaṣāyasvādulavaṇo guruḥ kāṇakapotakaḥ ||69|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.70"> raktapittapraśamanaḥ kaṣāyaviśado'pi ca | vipāke
                        madhuraścāpi guruḥ pārāvataḥ smṛtaḥ ||70|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.71"> kuliṅgo madhuraḥ snigdhaḥ kaphaśukravivardhanaḥ |71|
                        raktapittaharo veśmakuliṅgastvatiśukralaḥ ||71|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.72">
                        siṃhavyāghravṛkatarakṣvṛkṣadvīpimārjāraśṛgālamṛgervārukaprabhṛtayo guhāśayāḥ
                        ||72|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.73"> madhurā guravaḥ snigdhā balyā mārutanāśanāḥ | uṣṇavīryā
                        hitā nityaṃ netraguhyavikāriṇām ||73|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.74">
                        kākakaṅkakuraracāṣabhāsaśaśaghātyulūkacilliśyenagṛdhraprabhṛtayaḥ prasahāḥ
                        ||74|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.75"> ete siṃhādibhiḥ sarve samānā vāyasādayaḥ |
                        rasavīryavipākeṣu viśeṣācchoṣiṇe hitāḥ ||75|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.76"> madgumūṣikavṛkṣaśāyikāvakuśapūtighāsavānaraprabhṛtayaḥ
                        parṇamṛgāḥ ||76|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.77"> madhurā guravo vṛṣyāścakṣuṣyāḥ śoṣiṇe hitāḥ |
                        sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāśca kāsārśaḥśvāsanāśanāḥ ||77|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.78">
                        śvāvicchalyakagodhāśaśavṛṣadaṃśalopākalomaśakarṇakadalīmṛgapriyakājagarasarpamūṣikanakulamahābabhruprabhṛtayo
                        bileśayāḥ ||78|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.79"> varcomūtraṃ saṃhataṃ kuryurete vīrye coṣṇāḥ pūrvavat
                        svādupākāḥ | vātaṃ hanyuḥ śleṣmapitte ca kuryuḥ snigdhāḥ
                        kāsaśvāsakārśyāpahāśca ||79|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.80"> kaṣāyamadhurasteṣāṃ śaśaḥ pittakaphāpahaḥ |
                        nātiśītalavīryatvādvātasādhāraṇo mataḥ ||80|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.81"> godhā vipāke madhurā kaṣāyakaṭukā smṛtā |
                        vātapittapraśamanī bṛṃhaṇī balavardhanī ||81|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.82"> śalyakaḥ svādupittaghno laghuḥ śīto viṣāpahaḥ | priyako
                        mārute pathyo'jagarastvarśasāṃ hitaḥ ||82|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.83"> durnāmāniladoṣaghnāḥ kṛmidūṣīviṣāpahāḥ | cakṣuṣyā
                        madhurāḥ pāke sarpā medhāgnivardhanāḥ ||83|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.84"> darvīkarā dīpakāśca teṣūktāḥ kaṭupākinaḥ |
                        madhurāścāticakṣuṣyāḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtramārutāḥ ||84|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.85"> aśvāśvataragokharoṣṭrabastorabhramedaḥpucchakaprabhṛtayo
                        grāmyāḥ ||85|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.86"> grāmyā vātaharāḥ sarve bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphapittalāḥ | madhurā
                        rasapākābhyāṃ dīpanā balavardhanāḥ ||86|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.87"> nātiśīto guruḥ snigdho mandapittakaphaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        chagalastvanabhiṣyandī teṣāṃ pīnasanāśanaḥ ||87|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.88"> bṛṃhaṇaṃ māṃsamaurabhraṃ pittaśleṣmāvahaṃ guru |88|
                        medaḥpucchodbhavaṃ vṛṣyamaurabhrasadṛśaṃ guṇaiḥ ||88|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.89"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyaviṣamajvaranāśanam | śramātyagnihitaṃ
                        gavyaṃ pavitramanilāpaham ||89|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.90"> aurabhravatsalavaṇaṃ māṃsamekaśaphodbhavam |90|
                        alpābhiṣyandyayaṃ vargo jāṅgalaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ||90|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.91"> dūre janāntanilayā dūre pānīyagocarāḥ | ye mṛgāśca
                        vihaṅgāśca te'lpābhiṣyandino matāḥ ||91|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.92"> atīvāsannanilayāḥ samīpodakagocarāḥ | ye mṛgāśca
                        vihaṅgāśca mahābhiṣyandinastu te ||92||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.93"> ānūpavargastu pañcavidhaḥ | tadyathā- kūlacarāḥ, plavāḥ,
                        koṣasthāḥ, pādino, matsyāśceti ||93|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.94"> tatra
                        gajagavayamahiṣarurucamarasṛmararohitavarāhakhaḍgigokarṇakālapucchakodranyaṅkvaraṇyagavayaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        kūlacarāḥ paśavaḥ ||94|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.185">keśyaṃ rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ kāśmaryaṃ phalamucyate |
                        kṣatakṣayāpahaṃ hṛdyaṃ śītalaṃ tarpaṇaṃ guru ||185||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.186"> rase pāke ca madhuraṃ khārjūraṃ raktapittanut |
                        bṛṃhaṇīyamahṛdyaṃ ca madhūkakusumaṃ guru | vātapittopaśamanaṃ phalaṃ
                        tasyopadiśyate ||186|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.187"> vātāmākṣoḍābhiṣukaniculapicunikocakorumāṇaprabhṛtīni

                        bṛṃhaṇānyanilaghnāni balyāni madhurāṇi ca ||188|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.189"> kaṣāyaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ kiñcittiktaṃ rucipradam |
                        hṛdyaṃ sugandhi viśadaṃ lavalīphalamucyate ||189|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.190"> vasiraṃ śītapākyaṃ ca sāruṣkaranibandhanam | viṣṭambhi
                        durjaraṃ rūkṣaṃ śītalaṃ vātakopanam ||190|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.191">vipāke madhuraṃ cāpi raktapittaprasādanan |191|
                        airāvataṃ dantaśaṭhamamlaṃ śoṇitapittakṛt ||191|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.192">śītaṃ kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ ṭaṅkaṃ mārutakṛdguru |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.193"> śamīphalaṃ guru svādu rūkṣoṣṇaṃ keśanāśanam | guru
                        śleṣmātakaphalaṃ kaphakṛnmadhuraṃ himam ||193|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.194"> karīrākṣikapīlūni tṛṇaśūnyaphalāni ca |
                        svādutiktakaṭūṣṇāni kaphavātaharāṇi ca ||194|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.195"> tiktaṃ pinttakaraṃ teṣāṃ saraṃ kaṭuvipāki ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.196"> āruṣkaraṃ tauvarakaṃ kaṣāyaṃ kaṭupāki ca | uṣṇaṃ

                        ca ||196|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.197"> karañjakiṃśukāriṣṭaphalaṃ jantupramehanut | aṅkolasya

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.198"> rūkṣoṣṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ pāke laghu vātakaphāpaham |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.202"> jātīkośo'tha karpūraṃ jātīkaṭukayoḥ phalam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.205"> priyālamajjā madhuro vṛṣyaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ | baibhītako

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.207">bījapūrakaśamyākamajjā kośāmrasambhavaḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.208"> yasya yasya phalasyeha vīryaṃ bhavati yādṛśam | tasya

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.209"> phaleṣu paripakvaṃ yadguṇavattadudāhṛtam |
                        bilvādanyatra vijñeyamāmaṃ taddhi guṇottaram | grāhyuṣṇaṃ dīpanaṃ taddhi

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.212"> pittaghnānyanilaṃ kuryustathā mandakaphāni ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.213"> pittaghnaṃ teṣu kūṣmāṇḍaṃ bālaṃ madhyaṃ kaphāvaham |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.214"> sarvadoṣaharaṃ hṛdyaṃ pathyaṃ cetovikāriṇām |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.215"> alāburbhinnaviṭkā tu rūkṣā gurvyatiśītalā |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.216"> trapusairvārukarkārukaśīrṇavṛntaprabhṛtīni ||216|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.217"> svādutiktarasānyāhuḥ kaphavātakarāṇi ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.218"> bālaṃ sanīlaṃ trapusaṃ teṣāṃ pittaharaṃ smṛtam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.219"> ervārukaṃ sakarkāru sampakvaṃ kaphavātakṛt | sakṣāraṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.220"> sakṣāraṃ madhuraṃ caiva śīrṇavṛntaṃ kaphāpaham |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.221">
                        pippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverārdrakahiṅgujīrakakustumburujambīrasumukhasurasārjakabhūstṛṇasugandhaka-
                        kāsamardakakālamālakuṭherakakṣavakakharapuṣpaśigrumadhuśigruphaṇijjhakasarṣaparājikākulāhalāvagutthagaṇḍīratilaparṇikā-

                        kṛtānneṣūpayujyante saṃskārārthamanekadhā ||222|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.223"> teṣāṃ gurvī svāduśītā pippalyārdrā kaphāvahā | śuṣkā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.224"> svādupākyārdramaricaṃ guru śleṣmapraseki ca | kaṭūṣṇaṃ
                        laghu tacchuṣkamavṛṣyaṃ kaphavātajit ||224|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.225"> nātyuṣṇaṃ nātiśītaṃ ca vīryato maricaṃ sitam |
                        guṇavanmaricebhyaśca cakṣuṣyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||225|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.226"> nāgaraṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ vipāke madhuraṃ kaṭu | vṛṣyoṣṇaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.227"> kaphānilaharaṃ svaryaṃ vibandhānāhaśūlanut | kaṭūṣṇaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.228">laghūṣṇaṃ pācanaṃ hiṅgu dīpanaṃ kaphavātajit | kaṭu

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.230.1"> kāravī karavī tadvadvijñeyā sopakuñcikā |230| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.235">kaphaghnā laghavo rūkṣāstīkṣṇoṣṇāḥ pittavardhanāḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.239"> citrakastilaparṇī ca kaphaśophahare laghū | varṣābhūḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.240"> kaṭutiktarasā hṛdyā rocanī vahnidīpanī | sarvadoṣaharā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.242">tridoṣaśamanaṃ śuṣkaṃ viṣadoṣaharaṃ laghu | viṣṭambhi

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.243"> puṣpaṃ ca patraṃ ca phalaṃ tathaiva yathottaraṃ te

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.244"> snigdhoṣṇatīkṣṇaḥ kaṭupicchilaśca guruḥ saraḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.246"> nātyuṣṇavīryo'nilahā kaṭuśca tīkṣṇo
                        gururnātikaphāvahaśca | balāvahaḥ pittakaro'tha kiñcit palāṇḍuragniṃ ca
                        vivardhayettu ||246||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.247"> snigdho ruciṣyaḥ sthiradhātukārī balyo'tha

                        kṣīrapalāṇḍuruktaḥ ||247||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.248"> kalāyaśākaṃ pittaghnaṃ kaphaghnaṃ vātalaṃ guru |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.249">
                        cuccūyūthikātaruṇījīvantībimbītikānadī(ndī)bhallātakacchagalāntrī-

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.250"> kaṣāyasvādutiktāni raktapittaharāṇi ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.251"> laghuḥ pāke ca jantughnaḥ picchilo vraṇināṃ hitaḥ |
                        kaṣāyamadhuro grāhī cuccūsteṣāṃ tridoṣahā ||251|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.252">cakṣuṣyā sarvadoṣaghnī jīvantī samudāhṛtā | vṛkṣādanī

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.253">kṣīravṛkṣotpalādīnāṃ kaṣāyāḥ pallavāḥ smṛtāḥ | śītāḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.256"> taṇḍulīyakopodakā'śvabalācillīpālaṅkyāvāstūkaprabhṛtīni

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.257"> sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi sakṣāramadhurāṇi ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.258"> madhuro rasapākābhyāṃ raktapittamadāpahaḥ | teṣāṃ
                        śītatamo rūkṣastaṇḍulīyo viṣāpahaḥ ||258|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.259"> svādupākarasā vṛṣyā vātapittamadāpahā | upodakā sarā
                        snigdhā balyā śleṣmakarī himā ||259|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.260"> kaṭurvipāke kṛmihā medhāgnibalavardhanaḥ | sakṣāraḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.261"> cillī vāstūkavajjñeyā pālaṅkyā taṇḍulīyavat |

                        baddhaviṇmūtramārutam ||261|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.262">
                        maṇḍūkaparṇīsaptalāsuniṣaṇṇakasuvarcalāpippalīguḍūcīgojihvā-
                        kākamācīprapunnāḍāvalgujasatīnabṛhatīkaṇṭakārikāphala-
                        paṭolavārtākakāravellakakaṭukikākebu(mbu)korubūkaparpaṭakakirātatikta-

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.263"> raktapittaharāṇyāhurhṛdyāni sulaghūni ca |
                        kuṣṭhamehajvaraśvāsakāsāruciharāṇi ca ||263|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.264"> kaṣāyā tu hitā pitte svādupākarasā himā | laghvī
                        maṇḍūkaparṇī tu tadvadgojihvikā matā ||264||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.265"> avidāhī tridoṣaghnaḥ saṅgrāhī suniṣaṇṇakaḥ | avalgujaḥ
                        kaṭuḥ pāke tiktaḥ pittakaphāpahaḥ ||265|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.266"> īṣattiktaṃ tridoṣaghnaṃ śākaṃ kaṭu satīnajam |
                        nātyuṣṇaśītaṃ kuṣṭhaghnaṃ kākamācyāstu tadvidham ||266||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.267"> kaṇḍūkuṣṭhakṛmighnāni kaphavātaharāṇi ca | phalāni
                        bṛhatīnāṃ tu kaṭutiktalaghūni ca ||267||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.268"> kaphapittaharaṃ vraṇyamuṣṇaṃ tiktamavātalam | paṭolaṃ
                        kaṭukaṃ pāke vṛṣyaṃ rocanadīpanam ||268||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.269"> kaphavātaharaṃ tiktaṃ rocanaṃ kaṭukaṃ laghu | vārtākaṃ
                        dīpanaṃ proktaṃ jīrṇaṃ sakṣārapittalam | tadvat karkoṭakaṃ vidyāt
                        kāravellakameva ca ||269|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.270"> āṭarūṣakavetrāgraguḍūcīnimbaparpaṭāḥ |
                        kirātatiktasahitāstiktāḥ pittakaphāpahāḥ ||270|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.271"> kaphāpahaṃ śākamuktaṃ varuṇaprapunāḍa(ṭa)yoḥ | rūkṣaṃ
                        laghu ca śītaṃ ca vātapittaprakopaṇam ||271|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.272"> dīpanaṃ kālaśākaṃ tu garadoṣaharaṃ kaṭu | kausumbhaṃ
                        madhuraṃ rūkṣamuṣṇaṃ śleṣmaharaṃ laghu ||272|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.273"> vātalaṃ nālikāśākaṃ pittaghnaṃ madhuraṃ ca tat |
                        grahaṇyarśovikāraghnī sāmlā vātakaphe hitā | uṣṇā kaṣāyamadhurā cāṅgerī
                        cāgnidīpanī ||273||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.274">
                        loṇikājātukatriparṇikāpattūrajīvakasuvarcalāḍuḍurakakutumbakakuṭhiñjarakuntalikākuraṇṭikāprabhṛtayaḥ
                        ||274|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.275"> svādupākarasāḥ śītāḥ kaphaghnā nātipittalāḥ |
                        lavaṇānurasā rūkṣāḥ sakṣārā vātalāḥ sarāḥ ||275|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.276"> svādutiktā kuntalikā kaṣāyā sakuraṇṭikā |276| saṅgrāhi
                        śītalaṃ cāpi laghu doṣāpahaṃ tathā | rājakṣavakaśākaṃ tu śaṭīśākaṃ ca
                        tadvidham ||276|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.277"> svādupākarasaṃ śākaṃ durjaraṃ harimanthajam |277|
                        bhedanaṃ madhuraṃ rūkṣaṃ kālāyamativātalam ||277|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.278"> sraṃsanaṃ kaṭukaṃ pāke laghu vātakaphāpaham |
                        śophaghnamuṣṇavīryaṃ ca patraṃ pūtikarañjajam ||278|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.279"> tāmbūlapatraṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ kaṭu pittaprakopaṇam |
                        sugandhi viśadaṃ tiktaṃ svaryaṃ vātakaphāpaham ||279|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.280"> sraṃsanaṃ kaṭukaṃ pāke kaṣāyaṃ vahnidīpanam |
                        vaktrakaṇḍūmalakledadaurgandhyādiviśodhanam ||280|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.281"> atha puṣpavargaḥ | kovidāraśaṇaśālmalīpuṣpāṇi madhurāṇi
                        madhuravipākāni raktapittaharāṇi ca; vṛṣāgastyayoḥ puṣpāṇi tiktāni
                        kaṭuvipākāni kṣayakāsāpahāni ca ||281|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.282"> āgastyaṃ nātiśītoṣṇaṃ naktāndhānāṃ praśasyate ||282|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.283"> karīrakusumāni kaṭuvipākāni vātaharāṇi
                        sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ca ||283|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.284"> raktavṛkṣasya nimbasya muṣkakārkāsanasya ca |
                        kaphapittaharaṃ puṣpaṃ kuṣṭhaghnaṃ kuṭajasya ca ||284|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.285"> satiktaṃ madhuraṃ śītaṃ padmaṃ pittakaphāpaham |
                        madhuraṃ picchilaṃ snigdhaṃ kumudaṃ hlādi śītalam | tasmādalpāntaraguṇe
                        vidyāt kuvalayotpale ||285|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.286"> sindhuvāraṃ vijānīyāddhimaṃ pittavināśanam |286|
                        mālatīmallike tikte saurabhyāt pittanāśane ||286|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.287"> sugandhi viśadaṃ hṛdyaṃ bākulaṃ pāṭalāni ca |
                        śleṣmapittaviṣaghnaṃ tu nāgaṃ tadvacca kuṅkumam ||287|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.288"> campakaṃ raktapittaghnaṃ śītoṣṇaṃ kaphanāśanam |
                        kiṃśukaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ tadvadeva kuraṇṭakam ||288|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.289"> yathāvṛkṣaṃ vijānīyāt puṣpaṃ vṛkṣocitaṃ tathā |289|
                        madhuśigrukarīrāṇi kaṭūni śleṣmaharāṇi ca ||289|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.290"> kṣavakakulevaravaṃśakarīraprabhṛtīni kaphakarāṇi
                        sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ca ||290|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.291"> kṣavakaṃ kṛmilaṃ teṣu svādupākaṃ sapicchalam | visyandi
                        vātalaṃ nātipittaśleṣmakaraṃ ca tat ||291|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.292"> veṇoḥ karīrāḥ kaphalā madhurā rasapākataḥ | vidāhino
                        vātakarāḥ sakaṣāyā virūkṣaṇāḥ ||292|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.293"> udbhidāni palālekṣukarīṣaveṇukṣitijāni | tatra
                        palālajātaṃ madhuraṃ madhuravipākaṃ rūkṣaṃ doṣapraśamanaṃ ca | ikṣujaṃ
                        madhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ kaṭupākaṃ śītalaṃ ca | tadvadevoṣṇaṃ kārīṣaṃ kaṣāyaṃ
                        vātakopanaṃ ca, (veṇujātaṃ kaṣāyaṃ vātakopanaṃ ca,) bhūmijaṃ guru
                        nātivātalaṃ bhūmitaścāsyānurasaḥ ||293|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.294"> piṇyākatilakalkasthūṇikāśuṣkaśākāni
                        sarvadoṣaprakopaṇāni ||294|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.295"> viṣṭambhinaḥ smṛtāḥ sarve vaṭakā vātakopanāḥ |295|
                        siṇḍākī vātalā sārdrā ruciṣyā'naladīpanī ||295|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.296"> viḍbhedi guru rūkṣaṃ ca prāyo viṣṭambhi durjaram |
                        sakaṣāyaṃ ca sarvaṃ hi svādu śākamudāhṛtam | puṣpaṃ patraṃ phalaṃ nālaṃ
                        kandāśca guravaḥ kramāt ||296|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.297"> karkaśaṃ parijīrṇaṃ ca kṛmijuṣṭamadeśajam | varjayet

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.298"> atha kandavargaḥ | kandānāta ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ-

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.300"> madhuro bṛṃhaṇo vṛṣyaḥ śītaḥ svaryo'timūtralaḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.301"> vātapittaharī vṛṣyā svādutiktā śatāvarī | mahatī caiva

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.302"> grahaṇyarśovikāraghnī vṛṣyā śītā rasāyanī |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.303"> avidāhi bisaṃ proktaṃ raktapittaprasādanam | viṣṭambhi

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.304"> gurū viṣṭambhiśītau ca śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukau | piṇḍālukaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.305"> surendrakandaḥ śleṣmaghno vipāke kaṭu pittakṛt |305|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.307"> māna(ṇa)kaṃ svādu śītaṃ ca guru cāpi prakīrtitam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.338">śarkarekṣuvikāreṣu, pāne madhvāsavau tathā |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.339"> aparyuṣitamannaṃ tu saṃskṛtaṃ mātrayā śubham | phalaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.340"> atha kṛtānnavargaḥ | ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.361.1">| āpyāyanaḥ saṃhananaḥ śukrado balavardhanaḥ |361| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.361.2"> sa dāḍimayuto vṛṣyaḥ saṃskṛto doṣanāśanaḥ ||361|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.419"> ataḥ sarvānupānānyupadekṣyāmaḥ | - amlena kecidvihatā

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.424"> anupānaṃ vadantyeke taile yūṣāmlakāñjikam | śītodakaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.429">surā kṛśānāṃ sthūlānāmanupānaṃ madhūdakam | nirāmayānāṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.430"> snigdhoṣṇaṃ mārute pathyaṃ, kaphe rūkṣoṣṇamiṣyate |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.431">hitaṃ śoṇitapittibhyaḥ kṣīramikṣurasastathā |
                        arkaśeluśirīṣāṇāmāsavāstu viṣārtiṣu ||431|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432"> ataḥ paraṃ tu vargāṇāmanupānaṃ pṛthak pṛthak |
                        pravakṣyāmyanupūrveṇa sarveṣāmeva me śṛṇu ||432||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.433"> tatra pūrvaśasyajātānāṃ badarāmlaṃ, vaidalānāṃ
                        dhānyāmlaṃ, jaṅghālānāṃ dhanvajānāṃ ca pippalyāsavaḥ, viṣkirāṇāṃ
                        kolabadarāsavaḥ, pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛkṣāsavaḥ, guhāśayānāṃ
                        kharjūranālikerāsavaḥ, prasahānāmaśvagandhāsavaḥ, parṇamṛgāṇāṃ
                        kṛṣṇagandhāsavaḥ, bileśayānāṃ phalāsavaḥ , ekaśaphānāṃ triphalāsavaḥ,
                        anekaśaphānāṃ khadirāsavaḥ, kūlacarāṇāṃ śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukāsavaḥ, kośavāsināṃ
                        pādināṃ ca sa eva, plavānāmikṣurasāsavaḥ, nādeyānāṃ matsyānāṃ mṛṇālāsavaḥ,
                        sāmudrāṇāṃ mātuluṅgāsavaḥ, amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ, kaṣāyāṇāṃ
                        dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ, madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khaṇḍāsavaḥ, tālaphalādīnāṃ
                        dhānyāmlaṃ, kaṭukānāṃ dūrvānalavetrāsavaḥ, pippalyādīnāṃ
                        śvadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ, kūṣmāṇḍādīnāṃ dārvīkarīrāsavaḥ, cuccuprabhṛtīnāṃ
                        lodhrāsavaḥ, jīvantyādīnāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, kusumbhaśākasya sa eva,
                        maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnāṃ mahāpañcamūlāsavaḥ, tālamastakādīnāmamlaphalāsavaḥ,
                        saindhavādīnāṃ surāsava āranālaṃ ca, toyaṃ vā sarvatreti ||433|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.434"> bhavanti cātra- sarveṣāmanupānānāṃ māhendraṃ
                        toyamuttamam |434| sātmyaṃ vā yasya yattoyaṃ tattasmai hitamucyate ||434|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.435"> uṣṇaṃ vāte kaphe toyaṃ pitte rakte ca śītalam |435|

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.437">tarpaṇaṃ mārdavakaraṃ śramaklamaharaṃ sukham | dīpanaṃ

                        ||438||</l>
