                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.439.2"> sthiratāṃ gatamalkinnamannamadravapāyinām ||439|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.440.1"> bhavatyābādhajananamanupānamataḥ pibet |440| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.440.2"> na pibecchvāsakāsārto roge cāpyūrdhvajatruge ||440|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.441.1">kṣatoraskaḥ prasekī ca yasya copahataḥ svaraḥ |441| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.441.2"> pītvā'dhvabhāṣyādhyayanageyasvapnānna śīlayet ||441|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.442"> pradūṣyāmāśayaṃ taddhi tasya kaṇṭhorasi sthitam |
                        syandāgnisādacchardyādīnāmayāñjanayedbahūn ||442|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.443"> gurulāghavacinteyaṃ svabhāvaṃ nātivartate | tathā
                        saṃskāramātrānnakālāṃścāpyuttarottaram ||443|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.444"> mandakarmānalārogyāḥ sukumārāḥ sukhocitāḥ | jantavo ye
                        tu teṣāṃ hi cinteyaṃ parikīrtyate ||444|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.445"> balinaḥ kharabhakṣyā ye ye ca dīptāgnayo narāḥ |
                        karmanityāśca ye teṣāṃ nāvaśyaṃ parikīrtyate ||445|| ityanupānavargaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.446"> athāhāravidhiṃ vatsa! vistareṇākhilaṃ śṛṇu |446|
                        āptāsthitamasaṅkīrṇaṃ śuci kāryaṃ mahānasam ||446|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.447"> tatrāptairguṇasampannaṃ bhakṣyamannaṃ susaṃskṛtam |
                        śucau deśe susaṅguptaṃ samupasthāpayedbhiṣak ||447|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.448"> viṣaghnairagadaiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ prokṣitaṃ vyajanodakaiḥ |
                        siddhairmantrairhataviṣaṃ siddhamannaṃ nivedayet ||448|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.449"> vakṣyāmyataḥ paraṃ kṛtsnāmāhārasyopakalpanām | ghṛtaṃ
                        kārṣṇāyase deyaṃ, peyā deyā tu rājate ||449|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.450"> phalāni sarvabhakṣyāṃśca pradadyādvai daleṣu tu |
                        pariśuṣkapradigdhāni sauvarṇeṣu prakalpayet ||450|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.451">pradravāṇi rasāṃścaivaṃ rājateṣūpahārayet | kaṭvarāṇi
                        khaḍāṃścaiva sarvāñchaileṣu dāpayet ||451|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.452">dadyāttāmramaye pātre suśītaṃ suśṛtaṃ payaḥ | pānīyaṃ,
                        pānakaṃ madyaṃ mṛnmayeṣu pradāpayet ||452|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.453">kācasphaṭikapātreṣu śītaleṣu śubheṣu ca |
                        dadyādvaidūryacitreṣu rāgaṣāḍavasaṭṭakān ||453|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.454"> purastādvimale pātre suvistīrṇe manorame | sūdaḥ
                        sūpaudanaṃ dadyāt pradehāṃśca susaṃskṛtān ||454|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.455"> phalāni sarvabhakṣyāṃśca pariśuṣkāṇi yāni ca | tāni
                        dakṣiṇapārśve tu bhuñjānasyopakalpayet ||455|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.456"> pradravāṇi rasāṃścaiva pānīyaṃ pānakaṃ payaḥ | khaḍān
                        yūṣāṃśca peyāṃśca savye pārśve pradāpayet ||456|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.457">sarvān guḍavikārāṃśca rāgaṣāḍavasaṭṭakān | purastāt
                        sthāpayet prājño dvayorapi ca madhyataḥ ||457|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.458"> evaṃ vijñāya matimān bhojanasyopakalpanām | bhoktāraṃ
                        vijane ramye niḥsampāte śubhe śucau ||458|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.459"> sugandhapuṣparacite same deśe ca bhojayet |459|
                        viśiṣṭamiṣṭasaṃskāraiḥ pathyairiṣṭai rasādibhiḥ ||459|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.460"> manojñaṃ śuci nātyuṣṇaṃ pratyagramaśanaṃ hitam |460|
                        pūrvaṃ madhuramaśnīyānmadhye'mlalavaṇau rasau ||460|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.461"> paścāccheṣān rasān vaidyo bhojaneṣvavacārayet | ādau
                        phalāni bhuñjīta dāḍimādīni buddhimān ||461|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.462"> tataḥ peyāṃstato bhojyān bhakṣyāṃścitrāṃstataḥ param |
                        ghanaṃ pūrvaṃ samaśnīyāt, kecidāhurviparyayam ||462|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.463"> ādāvante ca madhye ca bhojanasya tu śasyate |
                        niratyayaṃ doṣaharaṃ phaleṣvāmalakaṃ nṛṇām ||463|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.464"> mṛṇālabisaśālūkakandekṣuprabhṛtīni ca | pūrvaṃ yojyāni
                        bhiṣajā na tu bhukte kadācana ||464|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.465"> sukhamuccaiḥ samāsīnaḥ samadeho'nnatatparaḥ | kāle
                        sātmyaṃ laghu snigdhamuṣṇaṃ kṣipraṃ dravottaram ||465|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.466"> bubhukṣito'nnamaśnīyānmātrāvadviditāgamaḥ |466| kāle
                        prīṇayate bhuktaṃ sātmyamannaṃ na bādhate ||466||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.467"> laghu śīghraṃ vrajet pākaṃ snigdhoṣṇaṃ balavahnidam |
                        kṣipraṃ bhuktaṃ samaṃ pākaṃ yātyadoṣaṃ dravottaram ||467||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.469"> sukhaṃ jīryati mātrāvaddhātusāmyaṃ karoti ca |468|
                        atīvāyatayāmāstu kṣapā yeṣvṛtuṣu smṛtāḥ ||468|| teṣu tatpratyanīkāḍhyaṃ
                        bhuñjīta prātareva tu | yeṣu cāpi bhaveyuśca divasā bhṛśamāyatāḥ ||469|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.470"> teṣu tatkālavihitamaparāhṇe praśasyate | rajanyo
                        divasāścaiva yeṣu cāpi samāḥ smṛtāḥ ||470||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.471"> kṛtvā samamahorātraṃ teṣu bhuñjīta bhojanam |471|
                        nāprāptātītakālaṃ vā hīnādhikamathāpi vā ||471|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.472">aprāptakālaṃ bhuñjānaḥ śarīre hyalaghau naraḥ | tāṃstān
                        vyādhīnavāpnoti maraṇaṃ vā niyacchati ||472|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.473">atītakālaṃ bhuñjāno vāyunopahate'nale |
                        kṛcchrādvipacyate bhuktaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca na kāṅkṣati ||473||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.474"> hīnamātramasantoṣaṃ karoti ca balakṣayam |
                        ālasyagauravāṭopasādāṃśca kurute'dhikam ||474|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.475"> tasmāt susaṃskṛtaṃ yuktyā doṣairetairvivarjitam |
                        yathoktaguṇasampannamupaseveta bhojanam ||475|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.476.1"> vibhajya doṣakālādīn kālayorubhayorapi |476| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.476.2"> acokṣaṃ duṣṭamutsṛṣṭaṃ pāṣāṇatṛṇaloṣṭavat ||476||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.477"> dviṣṭaṃ vyuṣitamasvādu pūti cānnaṃ vivarjayet |
                        cirasiddhaṃ sthiraṃ śītamannamuṣṇīkṛtaṃ punaḥ ||477|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.478.1">aśāntamupadagdhaṃ ca tathā svādu na lakṣyate |478| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.478.2"> yadyat svādutaraṃ tattadvidadhyāduttarottaram ||478|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.479"> prakṣālayedadbhirāsyaṃ bhuñjānasya muhurmuhuḥ |
                        viśuddhe rasane tasya rocate'nnamapūrvavat ||479||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.480"> svādunā tasya rasanaṃ prathamenātitarpitam | na tathā
                        svādayedanyattasmāt prakṣālyamantarā ||480|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.481"> saumanasyaṃ balaṃ puṣṭimutsāhaṃ harṣaṇaṃ sukham | svādu
                        sañjanayatyannamasvādu ca viparyayam ||481|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.482"> bhuktvā'pi yat prārthayate bhūyastat svādu bhojanam
                        |482| aśitaścodakaṃ yuktyā bhuñjānaścāntarā pibet ||482|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.483"> dantāntaragataṃ cānnaṃ śodhanenāharecchanaiḥ |
                        kuryādanirhṛtaṃ taddhi mukhasyāniṣṭagandhatām ||483|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.484"> jīrṇe'nne vardhate vāyurvidagdhe pittameva tu |
                        bhuktamātre kaphaścāpi,... |484| ... tasmādbhukteritaṃ kapham ||484|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.485"> dhūmenāpohya hṛdyairvā kaṣāyakaṭutiktakaiḥ |
                        pūgakaṅkolakarpūralavaṅgasumanaḥphalaiḥ ||485||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.486"> phalaiḥ kaṭukaṣāyairvā mukhavaiśadyakārakaiḥ |
                        tāmbūlapatrasahitaiḥ sugandhairvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||486|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.487"> bhuktvā rājavadāsīta yāvadannaklamo gataḥ | tataḥ
                        pādaśataṃ gatvā vāmapārśvena saṃviśet ||487|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.488"> śabdānrūpānrasān gandhān sparśāṃśca manasaḥ priyān |
                        bhuktavānupaseveta tenānnaṃ sādhu tiṣṭhati ||488|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.489"> śabdarūparasā gandhāḥ sparśāścāpi jugupsitāḥ |
                        aśucyannaṃ tathā bhuktamatihāsyaṃ ca vāmayet ||489|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.490"> śayanaṃ cāsanaṃ vā'pi necchedvā'pi dravottaram |
                        nāgnyātapau na plavanaṃ na yānaṃ nāpi vāhanam ||490|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.491"> na caikarasasevāyāṃ prasajyeta kadācana |
                        śākāvarānnabhūyiṣṭhamamlaṃ ca na samācaret ||491|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.492"> ekaikaśaḥ samastān vā nādhyaśnīyādrasān sadā |492|
                        prāgbhukte tvavivikte'gnau dvirannaṃ na samācaret ||492|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.493.1"> pūrvabhukte vidagdhe'nne bhuñjāno hanti pāvakam |493| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.493.2"> mātrāguruṃ pariharedāhāraṃ dravyataśca yaḥ ||493|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.494"> piṣṭānnaṃ naiva bhuñjīta mātrayā vā bubhukṣitaḥ |
                        dviguṇaṃ ca pibettoyaṃ sukhaṃ samyak prajīryati |494| peyalehyādyabhakṣyāṇāṃ
                        guru vidyādyathottaram ||494|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.495"> gurūṇāmardhasauhityaṃ laghūnāṃ tṛptiriṣyate |
                        dravottaro dravaścāpi na mātrāgururiṣyate ||495|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.496"> dravāḍhyamapi śuṣkaṃ tu samyagevopapadyate |496|
                        viśuṣkamannamabhyastaṃ na pākaṃ sādhu gacchati ||496|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.497"> piṇḍīkṛtamasaṅklinnaṃ vidāhamupagacchati |497|
                        srotasyannavahe pittaṃ paktau vā yasya tiṣṭhati ||497|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.498"> vidāhi bhuktamanyadvā tasyāpyannaṃ vidahyate |498|
                        śuṣkaṃ viruddhaṃ viṣṭambhi vahnivyāpadamāvahet ||498|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.499"> āmaṃ vidagdhaṃ viṣṭabdhaṃ kaphapittānilaistribhiḥ |
                        ajīrṇaṃ kecidicchanti caturthaṃ rasaśeṣataḥ ||499|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.500"> atyambupānādviṣamāśanādvā sandhāraṇāt
                        svapnaviparyayācca | kāle'pi sātmyaṃ laghu cāpi bhuktamannaṃ na pākaṃ
                        bhajate narasya ||500|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.501"> īrṣyābhayakrodhaparikṣatena lubdhena
                        śugdainyanipīḍitena | pradveṣayuktena ca sevyamānamannaṃ na samyak
                        pariṇāmameti ||501|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.502"> mādhuryamannaṃ gatamāmasañjñaṃ vidagdhasañjñaṃ
                        gatamamlabhāvam | kiñcidvipakvaṃ, bhṛśatodaśūlaṃ
                        viṣṭabdhamānaddhaviruddhavātam ||502|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.503"> udgāraśuddhāvapi bhaktakāṅkṣā na jāyate hṛdgurutā ca
                        yasya | rasāvaśeṣeṇa tu saprasekaṃ caturthametat pravadantyajīrṇam ||503|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.504"> mūrcchā pralāpo vamathuḥ prasekaḥ sadanaṃ bhramaḥ |
                        upadravā bhavantyete maraṇaṃ cāpyajīrṇataḥ ||504|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.505"> tatrāme laṅghanaṃ kāryaṃ, vidagdhe vamanaṃ hitam |
                        viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ pathyaṃ, rasaśeṣe śayīta ca ||505|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.506"> vāmayedāśu taṃ tasmāduṣṇena lavaṇāmbunā | kāryaṃ
                        vā'naśanaṃ tāvadyāvanna prakṛtiṃ bhajet ||506|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.507"> laghukāyamataścainaṃ laṅghanaiḥ samupācaret | yāvanna
                        prakṛtisthaḥ syāddoṣataḥ prāṇatastathā ||507||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.508"> hitāhitopasaṃyuktamannaṃ samaśanaṃ smṛtam | bahu
                        stokamakāle vā tajjñeyaṃ viṣamāśanam ||508|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.509"> ajīrṇe bhujyate yattu tadadhyaśanamucyate |
                        trayametannihantyāśu bahūnvyādhīnkaroti vā ||509|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.510"> annaṃ vidagdhaṃ hi narasya śīghraṃ śītāmbunā vai
                        paripākameti | taddhyasya śaityena nihanti pittamākledibhāvācca
                        nayatyadhastāt ||510|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.511"> vidahyate yasya tu bhuktamātre dahyeta hṛtkoṣṭhagalaṃ
                        ca yasya | drākṣābhayāṃ mākṣikasamprayuktāṃ līḍhvā'bhayāṃ vā sa sukhaṃ
                        labheta ||511|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.512"> bhaved ajīrṇaṃ prati yasya śaṅkā snigdhasya
                        jantorbalino'nnakāle | prātaḥ saśuṇṭhīmabhayāmaśaṅko bhuñjīta samprāśya
                        hitaṃ hitārthī ||512|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.513"> svalpaṃ yadā doṣavibaddhamāmaṃ līnaṃ na
                        tejaḥpathamāvṛṇoti | bhavatyajīrṇe'pi tadā bubhukṣā yā mandabuddhiṃ
                        viṣavannihanti ||513|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514"> ata urdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi guṇānāṃ karmavistaram |
                        karmabhistvanumīyante nānādravyāśrayā guṇāḥ ||514|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">hlādanaḥ stambhanaḥ śīto mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit |
                        uṣṇastadviparītaḥ syātpācanaśca viśeṣataḥ ||515|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">snehamārdavakṛt snigdho balavarṇakarastathā |
                        rūkṣastadviparītaḥ syādviśeṣāt stambhanaḥ kharaḥ ||516|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517"> picchilo jīvano balyaḥ sandhānaḥ śleṣmalo guruḥ |
                        viśado viparīto'smāt kledācūṣaṇaropaṇaḥ ||517|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518">dāhapākakarastīkṣṇaḥ srāvaṇo, mṛduranyathā |
                        sādopalepabalakṛdgurustarpaṇabṛṃhaṇaḥ ||518|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519"> laghustadviparītaḥ syāllekhano ropaṇastathā | daśādyāḥ
                        karmataḥ proktāsteṣāṃ karmaviśeṣaṇaiḥ ||519|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520"> daśaivānyān pravakṣyāmi dravādīṃstānnibodha me | dravaḥ
                        prakledanaḥ, sāndraḥ sthūlaḥ syādbandhakārakaḥ ||520|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521"> ślakṣṇaḥ picchilavajjñeyaḥ karkaśo viśado yathā |
                        sukhānubandhī sūkṣmaśca sugandho rocano mṛduḥ ||521|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.522"> durgandho viparīto'smāddhṛllāsārucikārakaḥ |
                        saro'nulomanaḥ prokto, mando yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||522|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.523"> vyavāyī cākhilaṃ dehaṃ vyāpya pākāya kalpate | vikāsī
                        vikasannevaṃ dhātubandhān vimokṣayet ||523|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.524"> āśukārī tathā''śutvāddhāvatyambhasi tailavat |
                        sūkṣmastu saukṣmyāt sūkṣmeṣu srotaḥsvanusaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||524|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525.1"> guṇā viṃśatirityevaṃ yathāvatparikīrtitāḥ |525| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525.2"> sampravakṣyāmyataścordhvamāhāragatiniścayam ||525|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526"> pañcabhūtātmake dehe hyāhāraḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ | vipakvaḥ
                        pañcadhā samyagguṇān svānabhivardhayet ||526|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527"> avidagdhaḥ kaphaṃ, pittaṃ vidagdhaḥ, pavanaṃ punaḥ |
                        samyagvipakvo niḥsāra āhāraḥ paribṛṃhayet ||527|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528"> viṇmūtramāhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ |528| sa tu
                        vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvān dhātūn pratarpayet ||528|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529"> kaphaḥ pittaṃ malaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syānnakharoma ca |
                        netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ ||529|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530"> divā vibuddhe hṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat |
                        annamaklinnadhātutvādajīrṇe'pi hitaṃ niśi ||530|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531"> hṛdi sammīlite rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ |
                        klinnavisrastadhātutvādajīrṇe na hitaṃ divā ||531|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532"> imaṃ vidhiṃ yo'numataṃ mahāmunernṛparṣimukhyasya
                        paṭheddhi yatnataḥ | sa bhūmipālāya vidhātumauṣadhaṃ mahātmanāṃ cārhati
                        sūrisattamaḥ ||532|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer"> iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ
                        tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā suśrutena viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo'dhyāyaḥ ||46|| </l>
                </div>
